The effect of revocation of approval of [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) is the automatic revocation of all work [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) that may have been issued based on such [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents).

### **§28-104.3 Amended Construction Documents**

Subject to the time limitations set forth in this code, amendments to approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) shall be submitted, reviewed and approved before the work or equipment is completed; and such amendments when approved shall be deemed part of the original [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents). The [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) may allow minor revisions of [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) to be made and submitted to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) after the completion of work but prior to [sign-off](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#sign-off) of the work in accordance with [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) rules.

### **§28-104.4 Place of Filing**

Except as otherwise provided by rule, applications for construction document approval shall be filed in the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) office in the borough in which the work or equipment is located or at the discretion of the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall be submitted electronically.

### **§28-104.5 Fees**

Filing fees shall be paid as required by [article 112](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#112).

### **§28-104.6 Applicant**

The applicant for approval of [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) shall be the [registered design professional](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#registered_design_professional) who prepared or supervised the preparation of the [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) on behalf of the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner).

**Exception:** The applicant may be other than a [registered design professional](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#registered_design_professional) for:

1. Limited oil burner/boiler [alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration), [limited plumbing alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#limited_plumbing_alterations), [limited sprinkler alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#limited_sprinkler_alterations), and [limited standpipe alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#limited_standpipe_alterations), where the applicant is licensed to perform such work pursuant to this code;
2. [Demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) applications other than those specified in [section 3306.5](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/33/safeguards-during-construction-or-demolition#3306.5) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014), where the applicant is the [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) contractor performing such [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition). In such cases, the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may require structural plans designed by a [registered design professional](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#registered_design_professional) to address any critical structural, sequencing or site safety items;
3. Elevator applications;
4. Applications for work falling within the practice of landscape architecture as defined by the New York state education law, including but not limited to landscaping and vegetation plans, tree protection plans, erosion and sedimentation plans, grading and drainage plans, curb cuts, pavement plans, and site plans for urban plazas and parking lots, where the applicant is a [landscape architect](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#landscape_architect). [Landscape architects](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#landscape_architect) shall not file plans for stormwater management and plumbing systems;
5. Other categories of work consistent with rules promulgated by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner).



#### **§28-104.6.1 Verification of Professional Qualification Required**

The [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall not accept [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) or other documents submitted in connection with applications for construction document approval or work [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) under this code by any person representing that he or she is a [registered design professional](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#registered_design_professional) or [landscape architect](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#landscape_architect) without verifying, by means of lists compiled and made available by the New York state [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of education pursuant to paragraph e-1 of subdivision four of section sixty-five hundred seven of the education law, that such person meets the qualifications established by law to practice as an [architect](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#architect) or [engineer](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#engineer) in New York state.

### **§28-104.7 Submittal of Construction Documents**

All [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) submitted to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall contain such information and shall be in such form as shall be set forth in this section 28-104.7 and the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). [Construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) shall also conform to standards as may be prescribed in the applicable sections of the construction codes.

#### **§28-104.7.1 Scope**

[Construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) shall be complete and of sufficient clarity to indicate the location and entire nature and extent of the work proposed, and shall show in detail that they conform to the provisions of this code and other applicable laws and rules; if there exist practical difficulties in the way of carrying out the strict letter of the code, laws or rules, the applicant shall set forth the nature of such difficulties.

#### **§28-104.7.2 Forms**

The applicant shall submit [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) on or accompanied by forms provided by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department).

#### **§28-104.7.3 Media**

[Construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) shall be printed upon suitable material, or presented as electronic media documents as determined by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner). Plans shall be drawn to suitable scale.

#### **§28-104.7.4 Quantities**

The applicant shall submit the number of copies of [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) as the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall require.

#### **§28-104.7.5 Citations to Code Sections Required**

In no case shall terms such as "code compliant", "approved", "legal" or similar terms be used in the [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) as a substitute for specific reference to a particular code section, approval or standard in order to show compliance with code requirements or other applicable laws and rules.

#### **§28-104.7.6 City Datum**

All elevations noted in the [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) shall be referred to and clearly identified as the North American vertical datum of 1988 ("NAVD") as established and maintained by National Geodetic Survey of the National Ocean Service, National Oceanic and Atmospheric Administration or successor agency, which is hereby established as the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) datum. Neither the United States coast and geodetic survey mean sea level datum of 1929 (national geodetic vertical datum, ("NGVD") nor any of the five borough data as established by the former Board of Estimate and Apportionment shall be referred to in [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) except as may be required for the purpose of demonstrating conversion to the NAVD. Conversions to NAVD shall be performed by [registered design professionals](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#registered_design_professional) or surveyors. Conversion to and from borough data and NGVD shall be performed using [tables 104.7.6.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#table_104.7.6.1) through 104.7.6.5.



| **BRONX ELEVATIONS** | **TO OBTAIN EQUIVALENCY:** | **NGVD ELEVATIONS** |
| -------------------- | -------------------------- | ------------------- |
| 10.000               | →add 2.608→                | 12.608              |
| 7.392                | →add 2.608→                | 10.000              |





| **BROOKLYN ELEVATIONS** | **TO OBTAIN EQUIVALENCY:** | **NGVD ELEVATIONS3** |
| ----------------------- | -------------------------- | -------------------- |
| 10.000                  | →add 2.547→                | 12.547               |
| 7.453                   | →add 2.547→                | 10.000               |





| **MANHATTAN ELEVATIONS** | **TO OBTAIN EQUIVALENCY:** | **NGVD ELEVATIONS** |
| ------------------------ | -------------------------- | ------------------- |
| 10.000                   | →add 2.752→                | 12.752              |
| 7.248                    | →add 2.752→                | 10.000              |





| **QUEENS ELEVATIONS** | **TO OBTAIN EQUIVALENCY:** | **NGVD ELEVATIONS** |
| --------------------- | -------------------------- | ------------------- |
| 10.000                | →add 2.725→                | 12.725              |
| 7.275                 | →add 2.725→                | 10.000              |





| **STATEN ISLAND ELEVATIONS** | **TO OBTAIN EQUIVALENCY:** | **NGVD ELEVATIONS** |
| ---------------------------- | -------------------------- | ------------------- |
| 10.000                       | →add 3.192→                | 13.192              |
| 6.808                        | →add 3.192→                | 10.000              |



#### **§28-104.7.7 Identification of Special and Progress Inspections**

Whenever work or [materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials) are subject to [special inspection](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection), as provided in this code, such work or [materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials) shall be listed on the title sheet of the [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents), or the sheet immediately following, as subject to special or [progress inspection](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#progress_inspection).

#### **§28-104.7.8 Identification of Materials**

[Construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) shall identify all [materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials) proposed to be used, including identification of the test standard to which they conform, and where applicable, supporting information or test data from the manufacturer attesting to such conformance.

#### **§28-104.7.9 Energy Conservation Code**

The application shall contain all information required to demonstrate compliance with the [New York city energy conservation code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-energy-conservation-code-2014). This information shall include signed and sealed construction drawings, including electrical drawings, to the extent that they demonstrate such [energy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#energy) code compliance, as required by such [energy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#energy) code and rules.

#### **§28-104.7.10 Preparer**

Each plan or drawing shall contain the [license](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#license) number, [seal](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#seal), signature (or equivalent as approved by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner)) and address of the [registered design professional](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#registered_design_professional) or [landscape architect](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#landscape_architect) who prepared or supervised the preparation of the plans.

#### **§28-104.7.11 Additional Information**

In addition to the data and information specified in this code and the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department), the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) is authorized to require the submission of additional plans, surveys, computations, analyses, test reports, photographs, [special inspection](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection) and such other data and information as may be necessary to determine compliance with this code and other applicable laws and rules.

#### **§28-104.7.12 Waiver of Certain Documents**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) is authorized to waive the submission of any of the required [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and other data if review of such documents is not necessary to ascertain compliance with this code or not required for the phase of work for which a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is sought.

#### **§28-104.7.13 Identification of Work Involving Raising or Moving a Building**

Where the lowest above-grade floor or the lowest subgrade floor of a building is to be raised, lifted, elevated or moved, such work shall be listed on the title sheet of the [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) as subject to [special inspection](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection).

#### **§28-104.7.14 Identification of Certain I-1 and I-2 Occupancies and of Certain Adult Homes, Enriched Housing, Community Residences and Intermediate Care Facilities as Exempt From Temporary External Generator Connection Requirements**

The title sheet of [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) for the following buildings shall list whether the building is exempt from the requirement to provide connections for temporary external generators pursuant to any exception contained in sections [G304.5.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/G/flood-resistant-construction#G304.5.1) or [G304.5.2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/G/flood-resistant-construction#G304.5.2) of appendix G of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014), as applicable:

1. A new or substantially improved building, as such term is defined in appendix G of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014), that contains [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space) classified in [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) group I-1 or I-2 or [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space) that is an adult home, enriched housing, community residence or intermediate care facility classified as [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) group R pursuant to an exception to [section 308.2.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/3/use-and-occupancy-classification#308.2.1) or [308.2.2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/3/use-and-occupancy-classification#308.2.2) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014), and that is located in an area of special flood hazard, as such term is defined in appendix G of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014); and
2. A new or substantially improved building that contains [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space) classified as an [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) group I-2 hospital and that is located in a shaded X-Zone, as such terms are defined in appendix G of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014).



#### **§28-104.7.15 Identification of Certain Hospitals as Exempt From Temporary External Boiler or Chiller Connection Requirements**

The title sheet of [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) for a new or substantially improved building, as such term is defined in appendix G of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014), that contains [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space) classified as an [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) group I-2 hospital and that is located in an area of special flood hazard or shaded X-Zone, as such terms are defined in appendix G of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014), shall list whether the requirement to provide connections for temporary external boilers and chillers pursuant to Item 2 of section G304.5.2 is inapplicable as a result of such building having its boiler and chiller plants located at or above the applicable design flood elevation.

#### ***§28-104.7.16 Tenant Protection Plan**

The title sheet of [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) shall contain a statement requiring a [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan to be submitted in accordance with the requirements of [article 120](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#120) prior to the issuance of a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration), construction or [partial demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition_partial) work in a building containing one or more occupied [dwelling units](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit).

*Section 28-104.7.16 was added by [Local Law 106 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll106of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of March 8, 2020.

### ***§28-104.8 Applications**

All applications shall comply with sections [28-104.8.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#*§28-104.8.1) through [28-104.8.3](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-104.8.3).

*Section 28-104.8 was amended by [Local Law 106 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll106of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of March 8, 2020.

#### ***§28-104.8.1 Applicant Statements**

The application shall contain the following signed and sealed statements by the applicant:

1. A statement certifying that the applicant is authorized by the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) to make the application and certifying that, to the best of the applicant's knowledge and belief, the [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) comply with the provisions of this code or the [1968 building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-1968-v1), if applicable, and other applicable laws and rules; if there exist practical difficulties in the way of carrying out the strict letter of the code, laws or rules, the applicant shall set forth the nature of such difficulties in such signed statement;
2. A [professional certification](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#professional_certification); and
3. A statement certifying compliance with the [New York city energy conservation code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-energy-conservation-code-2014).

*Section 28-104.8.1 was amended by [Local Law 106 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll106of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of March 8, 2020.

#### ***§28-104.8.2 Owner Statement**

The application shall contain a signed statement by the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner), and, in the case of cooperative or condominium forms of ownership, the application shall also contain a statement by the cooperative or condominium board, affirming that the applicant is authorized to make the application and, if applicable, acknowledging that construction and related documents will be accepted with less than full examination by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) based on the [professional certification](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#professional_certification) of the applicant. Such statement shall list the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner)'s full name and address, as well as the names of the principal officers, partners or other principals if a corporation, partnership or other entity. Principal officers of a corporation shall be deemed to include the president, vice presidents, secretary and treasurer. Where a current deed holder with a valid property interest or a court appointed entity or equivalent in charge of the property, or in the case of a cooperative or condominium unit, the cooperative or condominium board, notifies the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) in [writing](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#writing) that the applicant does not have authority to make the application, the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) is authorized pursuant to [section 28-104.2.10](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-104.2.10) to revoke approval of [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents). In addition, the application shall contain the following:

1. A signed statement certifying whether the building to be altered, constructed or demolished contains one or more occupied [dwelling units](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit);
2. A signed statement indicating whether the building to be altered, constructed or demolished contains housing accommodations subject to rent control or rent stabilization under chapters [3](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#3) and [4](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#4) of title 26 of the administrative code or rent regulation under Article 7-C of the [Multiple Dwelling Law](https://up.codes/viewer/ny-multiple-dwelling-law); and
3. If the building to be altered, constructed or demolished contains occupied housing accommodations subject to rent control under [chapter 3](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#3) of title 26 of the administrative code, the application shall contain a signed statement indicating that the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) has notified the New York state division of homes and community renewal that the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) has complied with all requirements imposed by the regulations of such agency as preconditions for such filing; or that the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) has not notified such agency because the nature and scope of the work proposed, pursuant to such regulations, does not require notification; or, if the building is subject to Article 7-C of the [Multiple Dwelling Law](https://up.codes/viewer/ny-multiple-dwelling-law), the application shall contain a signed statement indicating that the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) will notify the New York [City](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) Loft Board of the filing of the [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and will comply with all requirements imposed by [Multiple Dwelling Law](https://up.codes/viewer/ny-multiple-dwelling-law) Article 7-C and the Loft Board's rules.

*Section 28-104.8.2 was amended by [Local Law 106 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll106of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of March 8, 2020.

#### **§28-104.8.3 Information of Applicant, Filing Representative, and Owner**

The application shall set forth the full names, addresses, telephone numbers, and where available, e-mail addresses of the following persons and where any of such persons are corporations, partnerships or other business entities, the names and addresses of the principal officers, partners or other principals of such entity:

1. The applicant;
2. The filing representative;
3. The [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner), and, in the case of cooperative or condominium forms of ownership, cooperative [owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner)' corporation, or condominium [owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner)' association; and
4. Where a person other than the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) has engaged the applicant, such cooperative unit shareholder, condominium unit [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner), lessee, or mortgagee.



### **§28-104.9 Coastal Zones and Water-Sensitive Inland Zones**

[Construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) shall comply with sections [28-104.9.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-104.9.1) through [28-104.9.6](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-104.9.6) relating to work in [coastal zones and water-sensitive inland zones](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#coastal_zones_and_water-sensitive_inland_zones).

#### **§28-104.9.1 Definitions**

As used in [section 28-104.9](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-104.9) the following terms shall have the following meanings:

**[COASTAL AREAS OF SPECIAL FLOOD HAZARD](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#coastal_areas_of_special_flood_hazard).** Areas of land as identified on the flood insurance rate maps referenced in [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014) section G402 pursuant to article 36 of the New York state environmental conservation law.

**[COASTAL EROSION HAZARD AREAS](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#coastal_erosion_hazard_areas).** Areas of land as identified on the final map issued by the New York state [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of environmental conservation in accordance with section 34-0104 of the New York state environmental conservation law.

**[COASTAL ZONES AND WATER-SENSITIVE INLAND ZONES](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#coastal_zones_and_water-sensitive_inland_zones).** Areas of land comprising tidal [wetlands, freshwater](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#freshwater_wetlands) wetlands, [coastal erosion hazard areas](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#coastal_erosion_hazard_areas), [coastal areas of special flood hazard](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#coastal_areas_of_special_flood_hazard) or [rivervine and other inland areas of special flood hazard](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#rivervine_and_other_inland_areas_of_special_flood_hazard).

**[FRESHWATER WETLANDS](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#freshwater_wetlands).** Areas of land as identified on the final map issued by the New York state [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of environmental conservation in accordance with section 24-0301 of the New York state environmental conservation law, as well as any adjacent areas as such term is defined in section 662.1 of title six of the New York code of rules and regulations.

**[RIVERVINE AND OTHER INLAND AREAS OF SPECIAL FLOOD HAZARD](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#rivervine_and_other_inland_areas_of_special_flood_hazard).** Areas of land, including floodways, as identified on the flood insurance rate maps referenced in [section G402](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/G/flood-resistant-construction#G402) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014) pursuant to article 36 of the New York state environmental conservation law.

**STRUCTURE.** Any object constructed, installed or placed in, on or under land or water, including, but not limited to, a building, permanent shed, deck, in-ground or aboveground swimming pool, garage, mobile home, paving, road, public utility service distribution, transmission and collection system, storage tank, pier, dock, wharf, groin, jetty, seawall, revetment, bulkhead or breakwater.

**[TIDAL WETLANDS](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#tidal_wetlands).** Areas of land as identified on the tidal wetland inventory issued by the New York state [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of environmental conservation in accordance with section 25-0201 of the New York state environmental conservation law, as well as any adjacent areas as such term is defined in section 661.4 of title six of the New York code of rules and regulations.

#### **§28-104.9.2 Statement and Submission by Applicant**

It shall be the duty of an applicant for construction document approval to determine whether the proposed work is located within a coastal zone or a water-sensitive inland zone subject to [section 28-104.9.3](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-104.9.3) and/or [section 28-104.9](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-104.9). Applications for construction document approval shall include a statement by the applicant indicating whether the proposed work is located within a coastal zone or water-sensitive inland zone subject to such sections. The failure to disclose that proposed work is within a coastal zone or water-sensitive inland zone subject to such sections shall be a violation of this code.

#### **§28-104.9.3 Coordination With Department of Environmental Conservation and Other Agencies**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall not approve [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) for construction of a new structure, the horizontal [enlargement](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#enlargement) of a structure or to excavate or fill any land, within a tidal wetland, a tidal wetland adjacent area, freshwater wetland, freshwater wetland adjacent area, or coastal erosion hazard area, without documentation satisfactory to the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) that the New York state [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of environmental conservation, and such other governmental agencies as are applicable, have issued any applicable [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) or other approvals for such construction, excavation or fill.

#### **§28-104.9.4 Compliance With Special Flood Hazard Area Requirements Mandated Within Special Flood Hazard Areas**

Within [coastal areas of special flood hazard](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#coastal_areas_of_special_flood_hazard) and areas of special flood hazard, the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall not approve [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) for construction or [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) of buildings or structures, including [alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) pursuant to [section 28-101.4.3](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-101.4.3), or for any other activity regulated by [section G201](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/G/flood-resistant-construction#G201) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014), unless the application complies with the requirements of appendix G of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014).

#### **§28-104.9.5 False Statement or Omission**

No person shall submit an application for construction document approval for any structure within a coastal zone or water-sensitive inland zone which falsely avers or by omission causes the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) to determine that the subject property is not located within such zone or that the New York state [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of environmental conservation and other appropriate agencies have issued the appropriate [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) or approvals when they did not.

#### **§28-104.9.6 Revocation of Approval of Construction Documents**

Where the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) determines that work is located within a coastal zone or water-sensitive inland zone after [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) have been approved for such work and/or that the documentation required by sections [28-104.9.2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-104.9.2) through [28-104.9.4](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-104.9.4) has not been submitted, the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall revoke such approval and any associated work [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) that may have been issued for such work in accordance with [section 28-104.2.10](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-104.2.10).

### **§28-104.10 Construction Documents for Sites Near Subways or Tunnels**

[Construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) shall not be approved unless all applicable agency approvals regarding nearby subways or tunnels as provided for in sections [3304.3.3](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/33/safeguards-during-construction-or-demolition#3304.3.3) and [3304.3.5](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/33/safeguards-during-construction-or-demolition#3304.3.5) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014) have been submitted to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department).

### ***\*§28-104.11 Construction Documents for Sites That Are Covered Development Projects as Defined in Section 24-541 of the Administrative Code**

Construction documentsfor sites that are covered development [projects](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#project) as defined in section 24-541 of the administrative code shall comply with [section 28-104.11.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#**§28-104.11.1) through [28-104.11.4](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#*§28-104.11.4).

*Section 28-104.11 was added by [Local Law 97 of 2017](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll97of2017.pdf).This law has an effective date of June 1, 2019.

**Section 28-104.11 was amended by Local Law 91 of 2020. This law has an effective date of March 26, 2021.

#### ***\*§28-104.11.1 Definitions**

As used in this code in connection with provisions relating to the jurisdiction of the development of environmental protection, the terms covered development [project](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#project), development activity, post-construction stormwater management facility, stormwater construction [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit), stormwater maintenance [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit), and stormwater pollution prevention plan or SWPPP shall have the same definitions as such terms are def[ined in subchapter 1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#1) of chapter 5-A of title 24 of the administrative code.

*Section 28-104.11.1 was added by [Local Law 97 of 2017](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll97of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of June 1, 2019.

**Section 28-104.11.1 was amended by [Local Law 91 of 2020](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll91of2020.pdf). This law has an effective date of March 26, 2021.

#### ***\*§28-104.11.2 Disclosure Required**

It shall be the duty of an applicant for construction document approved to determine whether the site of the proposed work is part of a covered development [project](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#project) and to disclose such information on [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents). Failure to disclose such information on [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) shall be a violation of this code.

*Section 28-104.11.2 was added by [Local Law 97 of 2017](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll97of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of June 1, 2019.

**Section 28-104.11.2 was amended by [Local Law 91 of 2020](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll91of2020.pdf). This law has an effective date of March 26, 2021.

#### ***§28-104.11.3 Required Documentation**

Applications for construction document approval shall include copies of any required stormwater construction [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) issued by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of environmental protection and the stormwater pollution prevention plan for the covered development [project](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#project).

*Section 28-104.11.3 was added by [Local Law 97 of 2017](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll97of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of June 1, 2019.

#### ***§28-104.11.4 Revocation of Approval of Construction Documents**

Where the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) finds after the approval of [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) that the applicant failed to disclose the information required by this section, the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) may revoke such approval and any associated work [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) in accordance with the provisions of sections [28-104.2.10](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-104.2.10) and [28-104.2.10.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-104.2.10.1).

*Section 28-104.11.4 was added by [Local Law 97 of 2017](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll97of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of June 1, 2019.

## **Article 105 Permits**

### **§28-105.1 General**

It shall be unlawful to construct, enlarge, alter, repair, move, demolish, remove or change the use or [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) of any building or structure in the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city), to change the use or [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) of an open lot or portion thereof, or to erect, install, alter, repair, or use or operate any [sign](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign) or [service equipment](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#service_equipment) in or in connection therewith, or to erect, install, alter, repair, remove, convert or replace any gas, mechanical, plumbing, fire suppression or fire protection system in or in connection therewith or to cause any such work to be done unless and until a written [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) therefore shall have been issued by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) in accordance with the requirements of this code, subject to such exceptions and exemptions as may be provided in [section 28-105.4](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#*§28-105.4).

#### **§28-105.1.1 Notification to Fire Department**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner), in consultation with the fire [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner), shall establish a procedure for notifying the fire [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of the issuance of any [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) that will result in the issuance of a new or amended certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) or other change in the use or [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) of the [premises](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#premises). In no instance shall the required notice be given to the fire [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) more than one business day after the date of the issuance of the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit).

#### ***§28-105.1.2 Denial of Permits for Certain Arrears**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall not issue a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for a new building, [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition), place of assembly or major [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) that will change the use, egress or [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) for a property if $25,000 or more in covered arrears is owed to the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) with respect to such property or if the [owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of such property owe, in aggregate, $25,000 or more in covered arrears to the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city), provided that, where a [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) within a property is owned as a condominium or held by a shareholder of a [cooperative corporation](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#cooperative_corporation) under a proprietary lease, covered arrears owed to the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) for such unit shall not be considered covered arrears owed to the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) for such property. For the purposes of this section, the term "covered arrears" may include any of the following, but shall not include any such items that are currently in the appeals process:

1. Unpaid fines, civil penalties or judgments entered by a court of competent jurisdiction or the environmental control board pursuant to [chapter 2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/2/enforcement#2) of this title or [chapter 2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/2/enforcement#2) of title 28 of the code; and
2. Unpaid and past due fees or other charges lawfully assessed by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner).


**Exceptions**:

1. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may issue a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for a property if the applicant submits a certification from the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of finance that binding agreements are in force requiring payment of all covered arrears owed by the [owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of such property, and such [owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) are in compliance with such agreement.
2. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may issue a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for a property where the issuance of such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is necessary to correct an outstanding violation of this code, the housing maintenance code or any other applicable provisions of law or rule or where the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) determines that issuance of such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is necessary to perform work to protect public health and safety.
3. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may issue a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for a portion of a property occupied by a [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) who is not an [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of such property or responsible for any covered arrears owed with respect to such property.
4. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may issue a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit), for a [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) within a property that is owned by a condominium or held by a shareholder of a [cooperative corporation](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#cooperative_corporation) under a proprietary lease, if the [owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of record for such unit do not owe, in aggregate, $25,000 or more in covered arrears to the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city).
5. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may issue a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) where a property was the subject of an in rem foreclosure judgment in favor of the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) and was transferred by the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) to a third party pursuant to section 11-412.1 of the code.
6. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may issue a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) where a property is the subject of a court order appointing an administrator pursuant to article 7-a of the real property actions and proceedings law in a case brought by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of housing preservation and development.
7. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may issue a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) where a property is the subject of a loan provided by or through the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of housing preservation and development or the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) housing development corporation for the purpose of rehabilitation that has closed within the five years preceding the application for such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit).
8. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may issue a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for a property where the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of housing preservation and development or the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) housing development corporation notifies the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) that the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is required for participation in a program that involves rehabilitation of such property.


**Section 28-105.1.2 was amended by [Local Law 160 of 2017](http://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll160of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of December 28, 2017.*

#### ***§28-105.1.3 Denial of Permits for Excessive Violations**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall, no less than once every six months, compile a list of multiple dwellings that includes: (i) all multiple dwellings containing fewer than 35 units that have a ratio of open hazardous or immediately hazardous housing maintenance code violations or immediately hazardous or major construction code violations that equal in the aggregate three or more such violations for every [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) in such multiple dwelling; and (ii) all multiple dwellings containing 35 units or more that have a ratio of open hazardous or immediately hazardous housing maintenance code violations or immediately hazardous or major construction code violations that equal in the aggregate two or more such violations for every [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) in such multiple dwelling. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall not issue [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for multiple dwellings on such list. If the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of a multiple dwelling on such list corrects open hazardous or immediately hazardous housing maintenance code violations or immediately hazardous or major construction code violations in such multiple dwelling so that the ratio of such violations to the number of [dwelling units](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) in such multiple dwelling falls below those outlined in this section, the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall remove such multiple dwelling from such list. Such denial shall not apply where a [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) within such multiple dwelling is owned as a condominium or held by a shareholder of a [cooperative corporation](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#cooperative_corporation) under a proprietary lease.
Exceptions:

1. Where the issuance of such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is necessary to correct an outstanding violation of this code, the housing maintenance code or any other applicable provisions of law or rule.
2. Where the issuance of such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is necessary to perform work to protect public health and safety.
3. For a portion of a property occupied by a [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) who is not an [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of such property or responsible for any existing violations in such property.
4. Where a property was the subject of an in rem foreclosure judgment in favor of the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) and was transferred by the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) to a third party pursuant to section 11-412.1 of the code.
5. Where a property is the subject of a court order appointing an administrator pursuant to article 7-a of the real property actions and proceedings law in a case brought by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of housing preservation and development.
6. Where a property is the subject of a loan provided by or through the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of housing preservation and development or the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) housing development corporation for the purpose of rehabilitation that has closed within the five years preceding the application for such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit).
7. For a property where the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of housing preservation and development or the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) housing development corporation notifies the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) that the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is required in connection with the implementation of a program of such [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) or corporation.


**Section 28-105.1.3 was added by [Local Law 104 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll104of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of January 4, 2020.*

#### ***§28-105.1.4 Denial of Permits for False Statements on Applications for Construction Document Approval**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall not issue a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for an occupied building for at least one year following the date of a determination by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) that a false statement about the [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) status of such building has been made in an application for construction document approval. Such denial shall not apply where a [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) within such multiple dwelling is owned as a condominium or held by a shareholder of a [cooperative corporation](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#cooperative_corporation) under a proprietary lease.
Exceptions:

1. Where the issuance of such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is necessary to correct an outstanding violation of this code, the housing maintenance code or any other applicable provisions of law or rule.
2. Where the issuance of such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is necessary to perform work to protect public health and safety.
3. For a portion of a property occupied by a [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) who is not an [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of such property or responsible for any existing violations in such property.
4. Where a property was the subject of an in rem foreclosure judgment in favor of the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) and was transferred by the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) to a third party pursuant to section 11-412.1 of the code.
5. Where a property is the subject of a court order appointing an administrator pursuant to article 7-a of the real property actions and proceedings law in a case brought by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of housing preservation and development.
6. Where a property is the subject of a loan provided by or through the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of housing preservation and development or the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) housing development corporation for the purpose of rehabilitation that has closed within the five years preceding the application for such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit).
7. For a property where the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of housing preservation and development or the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) housing development corporation notifies the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) that the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is required in connection with the implementation of a program of such [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) or corporation.


**Section 28-105.1.4 was added by [Local Law 114 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll114of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of December 5, 2019.*

#### ***§28-105.1.5 Denial of Permits for Work Without Permit on Occupied Building**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall not issue a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for a building for at least one year following the date of a determination by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) that work has been performed without a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) in such building and such building was occupied at the time such work was being performed. Such denial shall not apply where a [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) within such multiple dwelling is owned as a condominium or held by a shareholder of a [cooperative corporation](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#cooperative_corporation) under a proprietary lease.
Exceptions:

1. Where the issuance of such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is necessary to correct an outstanding violation of this code, the housing maintenance code or any other applicable provisions of law or rule.
2. Where the issuance of such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is necessary to perform work to protect public health and safety.
3. For a portion of a property occupied by a [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) who is not an [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of such property or responsible for any existing violations in such property.
4. Where a property was the subject of an in rem foreclosure judgment in favor of the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) and was transferred by the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) to a third party pursuant to section 11-412.1 of the code.
5. Where a property is the subject of a court order appointing an administrator pursuant to article 7-a of the real property actions and proceedings law in a case brought by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of housing preservation and development.
6.
