Where a property is the subject of a loan provided by or through the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of housing preservation and development or the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) housing development corporation for the purpose of rehabilitation that has closed within the five years preceding the application for such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit).
7. For a property where the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of housing preservation and development or the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) housing development corporation notifies the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) that the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is required in connection with the implementation of a program of such [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) or corporation.


**Section 28-105.1.5 was added by [Local Law 114 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll114of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of December 5, 2019.*

### ***§28-105.2 Classification of Work Permits**

For the purposes of this code, work [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be classified as follows:

1. **New building [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit):** for the construction of new buildings, including as provided for in [section 28-101.4.5](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-101.4.5).
2. **[Alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit):** for the [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) of buildings or structures, including new and existing [sign](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign) structures and [partial demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition_partial) in conjunction with such buildings or structures.
3. **Foundation and earthwork [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit):** for the construction or [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) of foundations, including earthwork, excavation, fill, and foundation insulation.
4. **Earthwork [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit):** for work solely involving earthwork, excavation, or fill operations.
5. **[Full demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition_full) [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit):** for the [full demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition_full) and removal of buildings or structures.
6. **Plumbing [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit):** for the installation or [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) of plumbing and plumbing systems, including gas piping. Such [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall include [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for [limited plumbing alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#limited_plumbing_alterations).
7. **[Sign](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign) [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit):** for the erection, installation or [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) of [signs](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign).
8. **[Service equipment](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#service_equipment) [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit):** for the installation or [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) of [service equipment](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#service_equipment), including but not limited to air conditioning and ventilating systems, boilers, elevators, escalators, moving walkways, dumbwaiters, mobile boilers and mobile oil tanks. Such [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall include [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for limited oil burner/boiler [alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration).
9. **Temporary construction equipment [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit):** for the erection, installation and use of temporary structures to facilitate construction and/or safety during construction, including but not limited to temporary fences, railings, catch platforms, over-the-sidewalk chutes, footbridges, sidewalk sheds, and scaffolds.
10. **Fire protection and suppression system [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit):** for the installation and [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) of fire protection and suppression systems, including sprinkler systems and standpipe systems. Such [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall include [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for [limited sprinkler alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#limited_sprinkler_alterations) and limited standpipe [alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration).
11. **Crane and derrick [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit):** for the use of power operated cranes and derricks during construction.

**Section 28-105.2, Item #10 was amended by [Local Law 195 of 2018](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll195of2018.pdf). This law has an effective date of May 30, 2019.*

#### **§28-105.2.1 Submittal Documents Required for Foundations and Earthwork**

Prior to the issuance of any [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for work that includes foundations and/or earthwork, [submittal documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#submittal_documents) clearly illustrating support of excavation design, including but not limited to stepping, sheeting, sloping, shoring, and bracing, and any protective railings or equipment required by [chapter 33](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/33/safeguards-during-construction-or-demolition#33) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014) shall be required.

#### **§28-105.2.2 Submittal Documents Required for Partial Demolition**

Prior to the issuance of any [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for work that includes [partial demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition_partial), [submittal documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#submittal_documents) shall be required in accordance with [chapter 33](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/33/safeguards-during-construction-or-demolition#33) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014).

### **§28-105.3 Separate Permits Required**

Separate work [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be required, as provided above, except that separate [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for foundations and earthwork, or for the installation or [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) of air conditioning systems, ventilation systems, and heating systems shall not be required whenever such work is included in and forms a part of the [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) filed for the construction of a new building or the [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) of a building or structure.

### ***§28-105.4 Work Exempt From Permit**

Exemptions from [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) requirements of this code shall not be deemed to grant authorization for any work to be done in any manner in violation of the provisions of this code, the [zoning resolution](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-zoning-resolution) or any other law or rules enforced by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). Such exemptions shall not relieve any [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of the obligation to comply with the requirements of or file with other [city agencies](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#city_agency). Unless otherwise indicated, [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall not be required for the following:

1. Emergency work, as set forth in [section 28-105.4.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-105.4.1).
2. [Minor alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#minor_alterations) and [ordinary repairs](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#ordinary_repairs), as described in [section 28-105.4.2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-105.4.2).
3. Certain work performed by a public utility company or public utility corporation, as set forth in [section 28-105.4.3](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-105.4.3).
4. Ordinary [plumbing work](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#plumbing_work), as set forth in [section 28-105.4.4](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-105.4.4).
5. [Permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for the installation of certain [signs](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign), as set forth in [section 28-105.4.5](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-105.4.5).
6. Geotechnical investigations, as set forth in [section 28-105.4.6](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-105.4.6).
7. The installation, [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) or removal of alternative automatic fire extinguishing systems, including but not limited to fire extinguishing systems for commercial cooking equipment, subject to the approval of the fire [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) in accordance with section 105 of the *[New York city fire code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-fire-code-2014)*.
8. The installation, [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) or removal of fire alarm systems, emergency alarm systems and fire [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) in-building auxiliary radio communication systems, subject to the approval of the fire [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) in accordance with the requirements of this code. Such work shall be submitted in accordance with the rules and regulations of the fire [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department).
9. Other categories of work as described in [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) rules, consistent with public safety.

**Section 28-105.4 was amended by [Local Law 195 of 2018](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll195of2018.pdf). This law has an effective date of May 30, 2019.*

#### **§28-105.4.1 Emergency Work**

Work that would otherwise require a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) may be performed without a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) to the extent necessary to relieve an emergency condition. An application for a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be submitted within 2 business days after the commencement of the emergency work and shall include written description of the emergency condition and the measures undertaken to mitigate the hazard. Emergency work may include but shall not be limited to:

1. Erection of sidewalk sheds, fences, or other similar structures to protect the public from an unsafe condition.
2. Stabilization of unsafe structural conditions.
3. Repair of gas leaks.
4. Repair or replacement of heating or hot water equipment servicing residential [occupancies](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) during the heating season as established by the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) housing maintenance code or education [occupancies](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) between November 1st and May 1st.
5. Replacement of parts required for the operation of a combined standpipe or sprinkler system.



#### **§28-105.4.2 Minor Alterations and Ordinary Repairs**

A [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall not be required for [minor alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#minor_alterations) and [ordinary repairs](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#ordinary_repairs).

##### **§28-105.4.2.1 Definitions**

The following words and terms shall, for the purposes of this [section 28-105.4.2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-105.4.2) and as used elsewhere in this code, have the meanings shown herein.

**[MINOR ALTERATIONS](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#minor_alterations).** Minor changes or modifications in a building or any part thereof, excluding [additions](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#addition) thereto, that do not in any way affect health or the fire or structural safety of the building or the safe use and operation of the [service equipment](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#service_equipment) therein. [Minor alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#minor_alterations) shall not include any of the work described as "[work not constituting minor alterations or ordinary repairs](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#work_not_constituting_minor_alterations_or_ordinary_repairs)."

**[ORDINARY REPAIRS](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#ordinary_repairs).** Replacements or renewals of existing work in a building, or of parts of the [service equipment](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#service_equipment) therein, with the same or equivalent [materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials) or equipment parts, that are made in the ordinary course of maintenance and that do not in any way affect health or the fire or structural safety of the building or the safe use and operation of the [service equipment](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#service_equipment) therein. [Ordinary repairs](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#ordinary_repairs) shall include the repair or replacement of any plumbing fixture, piping or faucets from any exposed stop valve to the inlet side of a trap. [Ordinary repairs](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#ordinary_repairs) shall not include any of the work described as "[work not constituting minor alterations or ordinary repairs](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#work_not_constituting_minor_alterations_or_ordinary_repairs)."

**[WORK NOT CONSTITUTING MINOR ALTERATIONS OR ORDINARY REPAIRS](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#work_not_constituting_minor_alterations_or_ordinary_repairs).** [Minor alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#minor_alterations) or [ordinary repairs](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#ordinary_repairs) shall not include:

1. The cutting away of any load bearing or required fire rated wall, floor, or roof construction, or any portion thereof.
2. The removal, cutting, or modification of any beams or structural supports;
3. The removal, change, or closing of any required exit;
4. The [addition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#addition), rearrangement, relocation, removal or replacement of any parts of the building affecting loading or exit requirements, or light, heat, ventilation, or elevator requirements or accessibility requirements, or any fire suppression or fire protection system;
5. [Additions](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#addition) to, [alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) of, or rearrangement, relocation, replacement, repair or removal of any portion of a standpipe or sprinkler system, water distribution system, house sewer, private sewer, or drainage system, including leaders, or any soil, waste or vent pipe, or any gas distribution system;
6. Any [plumbing work](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#plumbing_work) other than the repair or replacement of plumbing fixtures, piping or faucets from the exposed stop valve to the inlet side of a trap;
7. The [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) or repair of a [sign](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign) for which a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is required; or
8. Any other work affecting health or the fire or structural safety of the building or the safe use and operation of the [service equipment](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#service_equipment) therein.



#### **§28-105.4.3 Public Utility Company or Public Utility Corporation**

A [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall not be required for:

1. The installation or [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) of gas service piping or gas [meter](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#meter) piping including [meters](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#meter), valves, regulators, and related equipment, when such work is to be performed and serviced and maintained by utility corporations subject to the jurisdiction of the New York state public service commission;
2. The emergency repair of gas distribution piping when such work is performed by licensed master plumbers or by utility corporations subject to the jurisdiction of the New York state public service commission, in order to alleviate hazardous conditions, provided that a written report describing the details of such repairs shall be filed with the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) upon completion of the work.



#### **§28-105.4.4 Ordinary Plumbing Work**

The following ordinary [plumbing work](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#plumbing_work) may be performed without a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit), provided that the licensed plumber performing such work: (i) provides a monthly report listing completed work and work in progress during the preceding month, including the block, lot and address of each job, a description of the work performed or in progress at each address, and the location in each building where the work was performed or is in progress; (ii) pays the fees for such work in accordance with this code; and (iii) submits to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) a certification that the work was performed in accordance with this code and all applicable laws and rules. Ordinary [plumbing work](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#plumbing_work) shall include:

1. The removal of a domestic plumbing system not connected to a fire suppression or fire protection system, or the removal of a portion of such system.
2. The relocation of up to two plumbing fixtures within the same room to a maximum of 10 feet (3048 mm) distant from the original location, except in health care facilities.
3. The installation, replacement or repair of a food waste grinder (food waste disposal) or secondary back flow preventer and the replacement or repair of a sump pump.
4. The replacement of closet bends.
5. In buildings in [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) group R-2 occupied by fewer than six families or in buildings in [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) group R-3, the replacement of a gas water heater or a gas fired boiler with a capacity of 350,000 BTU or less where the existing appliance gas cock is not moved, provided that the plumber has inspected the chimney and found it to be in good operational condition.
6. The repair or replacement of any non-gas, non-fire suppression piping not longer than 10 feet (3048 mm) inside a building, or connected piping previously repaired or replaced under this provision.
7. The repair or replacement of non-fire suppression branch piping after the riser shutoff valve, including the replacement of fixtures, limited to two bathrooms and one kitchen per building per monthly reporting period.
8. The replacement of flexible gas tubing no greater than 4 feet (1219 mm) in length located downstream of the existing gas cock to an appliance, provided such gas tubing does not penetrate a wall.



#### **§28-105.4.5 Sign Permits**

A [sign](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign) [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall not be required where the [sign](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign) is:

1. Painted directly on the exterior wall surface of a building or on the surface of a fence;
2. A wall [sign](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign) of not more than six square feet (0.56 m2) in area;
3. Erected by employees of a [city agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#city_agency), including traffic and other similar [signs](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign);
4. A ground [sign](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign) offering the sale or rental of the [premises](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#premises) on which it is erected, provided the [sign](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign) does not exceed 12 square feet (1.1 m2) in area;
5. Temporary and erected during construction work and related thereto;
6. Temporary for special decorative display use for holidays, public demonstrations, or the promotion of civic, welfare or charitable purposes, except that [signs](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign) that utilize streets or cross streets shall be subject to the requirements of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of transportation; or
7. Temporary [signs](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign) offering the sale or rental of real property when erected on the [premises](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#premises) offered for sale or rent.



#### **§28-105.4.6 Geotechnical Investigations**

A [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall not be required for excavation performed for a geotechnical investigation required by [section 1802.4](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/18/soils-and-foundations#1802.4) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014) provided such excavation does not exceed 10 feet (3048 mm) in length, width, or diameter and is conducted under the supervision of a [registered design professional](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#registered_design_professional). All excavation activity, including backfilling of excavations, shall comply with all relevant code provisions, including but not limited to sections [1803](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/18/soils-and-foundations#1803) and [3304](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/33/safeguards-during-construction-or-demolition#3304) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014).

### ***§28-105.5 Application for Permit**

All applications for [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be submitted on forms furnished by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). Applications shall include all information required by this code, other applicable law or the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). The applicant shall list any portions of the design that have been approved for [deferred submittal](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#deferred_submittal) in accordance with [section 28-104.2.6](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-104.2.6). The application shall set forth an inspection program for the [project](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#project). An application for a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be submitted no later than 12 months after the approval of all required [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) (other than those documents approved for [deferred submittal](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#deferred_submittal)). The [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall provide written notification to [owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of adjoining property at the time such application is submitted.

**Section 28-105.5 was amended by [New York State Laws of 2018 Chapter 217](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/nys_ch_217_adjoining_owner_notice.pdf). This law has an effective date of August 24, 2018.*

#### **§28-105.5.1 Applicant for Permit**

The applicant for a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be the person who performs the work or who retains a subcontractor to do the work.

**Exception:** For [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) issued for [plumbing work](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#plumbing_work), fire protection and suppression work, and oil burner/boiler work, the applicant for such [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be the licensed master plumber, licensed master fire suppression piping contractor, or licensed oil-burning equipment installer, respectively, who performs the work.

#### ***§28-105.5.1 Application for Permit Where a Building Is Occupied**

All applications for [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for work on a building having more than three dwelling shall state the total number of units, and the number of units occupied at the time the application is filed.

**[Section 28-105.5.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-105.5.1) was added by [Local Law 149 of 2017](http://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll149of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of December 28, 2017.*

#### ***§28-105.5.2 Owner Statement**

All applications for [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall include a certification by the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of the property for which the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is sought stating the following:

1. A statement as to whether $25,000 or more in covered arrears, that are not currently in the appeals process, are owed to the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) with respect to such property;

2. A statement as to whether the [owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of the property owe, in aggregate, $25,000 or more in covered arrears to the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city);

3. For each owner of the property:

   3.1 The person's full name and business address;

   3.2 A list of properties in the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) for which the person owes covered arrears to the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) and, for each such property, the amount of such covered arrears owed; and

   3.3 A list of properties in the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) for which the person is an [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner);

4. If an exception to [section 28-105.1.2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#*§28-105.1.2) of the code applies to such [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner), a description of such exception.


**Section 28-105.5.2 was added by [Local Law 160 of 2017](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll160of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of December 28, 2017.*

##### **§28-105.5.2.1 Audit**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall each year, in consultation with the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of finance and each other appropriate [city agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#city_agency), audit at least 25 percent of the statements submitted under [section 28-105.5.2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#*§28-105.5.2) of the code.

**Section 28-105.5.2.1 was added by [Local Law 160 of 2017](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll160of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of December 28, 2017.*

### **§28-105.6 Fees**

Applications for [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be accompanied by the payment of appropriate fees as provided for in [article 112](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#112).

### **§28-105.7 Time Limitation of Applications**

An application for a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be deemed to have been abandoned 12 months after the date of its submission, unless such application has been diligently prosecuted after rejection in whole or in part, or a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall have been issued except that the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may, for reasonable cause, and upon payment of all reinstatement fees as provided for in this code, grant extensions of time for additional 12-month periods.

### **§28-105.8 Validity of Permit**

The issuance or granting of a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall not be construed to be a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for, or an approval of, any violation of any of the provisions of this code or of any other law or rule. [Permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) presuming to give authority to violate or cancel the provisions of this code or other law or rule shall not be valid. The issuance of a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) based on [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and other data shall not prevent the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) from requiring the correction of errors in the [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and other data. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) is authorized to prevent any [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy), use or work in violation of this code, the [zoning resolution](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-zoning-resolution) or other law or rule enforced by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department).

#### **§28-105.8.1 Duration of Permit**

[Permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) may be issued for a period of up to two years unless otherwise limited by law.

#### **§28-105.8.2 Signature of Commissioner on Permit**

Every [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) issued by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall have his or her signature affixed thereto; but the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may authorize any subordinate to affix such signature, including by the use of electronic means.

### **§28-105.9 Expiration**

All [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) issued by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall expire by limitation and become invalid if the permitted work or use is not commenced within 12 months from the date of issuance of the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit). Subsequent to the 12-month period following the issuance of the initial [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit), all [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall expire if the permitted work is suspended or abandoned for a continuous period of 12 months unless such [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) expire earlier pursuant to applicable provisions of this code. The [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall automatically expire upon the expiration of required insurance or if the applicant holds a [license](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#license) issued by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) upon the expiration or revocation of such [license](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#license) during the term of the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit).

**Exception:** All [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for work in an area of special flood hazard shall comply with [section G104](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/G/flood-resistant-construction#G104) of appendix G of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014).

#### **§28-105.9.1 Reinstatement**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may at any time reinstate a work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) solely for the purpose of [sign-off](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#sign-off), including the correction of defects noted in a final inspection as provided in [section 28-116.2.4](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#*§28-116.2.4) of this code, or reinstate a work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) within a period of two years from the date of issuance of the original [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit). Except in the case of a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) reinstated solely for the purpose of [sign-off](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#sign-off), the work shall comply with all the requirements of this code and other applicable laws and rules in effect at the time application for reinstatement is made. The applicant for reinstatement shall pay all reinstatement fees as required by [article 112](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#112).

### **§28-105.10 Suspension or Revocation of Permit**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) is authorized to suspend or revoke a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) issued under the provisions of this code.

#### ***§28-105.10.1 Notice of Proposed Revocation**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may, on [written notice](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#written_notice) to the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) holder, revoke any [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for failure to comply with the provisions of this code or other applicable laws or rules; or whenever there has been any false statement or any misrepresentation as to a material fact in the application or [submittal documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#submittal_documents) upon the basis of which such approval was issued; or whenever a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) has been issued in error and conditions are such that the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) should not have been issued. Such notice may be accompanied by a stop work order pursuant to [section 28-207.2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/2/enforcement#*§28-207.2) of this code and shall inform the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) holder of the reasons for the proposed revocation and that the applicant has the right to present to the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) or his or her representative within 10 business days of delivery of the notice by hand or 15 calendar days of the posting of notice by mail, information as to why the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) should not be revoked.

*Section 28-105.10.1 was amended by [Local Law 62 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll62of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of September 27, 2019.

#### **§28-105.10.2 Immediate Suspension in Cases of Imminent Peril**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may immediately suspend any [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) without prior notice to the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) holder when the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) has determined that an imminent peril to life or property exists. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall forthwith notify the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) holder that the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) has been suspended and the reasons therefore, that it is proposed to be revoked, and that the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) holder has the right to present to the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) or his or her representative within 10 business days of delivery of the notice by hand or 15 calendar days of the posting of notice by mail information as to why the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) should not be revoked.

### ***§28-105.11 Posting of Permit**

The building [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) or a copy thereof shall be posted in a conspicuous place at the work site, visible to the public for the duration of the work, or the use and operation of the equipment, or until the expiration of the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit). No such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be posted or displayed at any location other than the location of the [premises](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#premises) or equipment for which the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) was issued. Where the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is exposed to the weather, it shall be laminated or encased in a plastic covering to protect it from the elements. The [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall identify whether any [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) within such building will be occupied during the work. If [dwelling units](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) within such building will be occupied during the work, the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall indicate the total number of [dwelling units](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) that will be occupied.


**Exception:** Where a [project](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#project) information panel is required by [section 3301.9.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/33/safeguards-during-construction-or-demolition#3301.9.1), of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014), the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be posted in accordance with such section, and no other [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be posted in any location readily visible to the public, except as provided in [section 3301.9.5](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/33/safeguards-during-construction-or-demolition#3301.9.5) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014).

**Section 28-105.11 was amended by [Local Law 158 of 2017](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll158of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of August 30, 2018.*

### **§28-105.12 Conditions of Permit**

[Permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be subject to the following conditions:

#### **§28-105.12.1 Compliance With Code**

[Permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be deemed to incorporate the provisions that the applicant, the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner), their agents, employees, and contractors shall carry out the permitted work in accordance with the provisions of this code and other applicable laws or rules, whether specified or not, except as variations have been legally permitted or authorized.

#### **§28-105.12.2 Compliance With Construction and Submittal Documents**

All work shall conform to the approved construction and [submittal documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#submittal_documents), and any approved amendments thereto. Changes and revisions during the course of construction shall conform to the amendment requirements of this code.

#### **§28-105.12.3 Adherence to Lot Diagram**

All work shall be strictly located in accordance with the lot diagram approved in accordance with this code and no lot or plot shall be changed, increased or diminished in area from that shown on the approved lot diagram, unless and until a revised diagram showing such changes, accompanied by the necessary statement of the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) or applicant, shall have been submitted to and approved by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner).

#### **§28-105.12.4 Compliance With Safety Requirements**

All work shall be conducted in accordance with and subject to the safety requirements of this code and other applicable laws or rules, including any order or requirement of the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) that the building or structure under construction or [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) be vacated, in whole or in part, during the progress of the work and until the issuance of a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy). Adjoining lots and properties shall be protected in accordance with this code.

#### **§28-105.12.5 Compliance With Noise Control Code Required**

All work shall be performed in compliance with the provisions of the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) noise control code as set forth in [chapter 2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/2/enforcement#2) of title 24 of the administrative code. Failure to comply with sections 24-222 and 24-223 of the administrative code shall be a violation of this code.

#### **§28-105.12.6 Deferred Submittals**

Where [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) are issued subject to [deferred submittal](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#deferred_submittal) of portions of the design as provided for in [section 28-104.2.6](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-104.2.6), the [deferred submittal](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#deferred_submittal) items shall not be installed until the construction and [submittal documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#submittal_documents) for such portions have been approved by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) and, where applicable, new or amended [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) have been issued.

#### **§28-105.12.7 Insurance**

Where workers compensation, employee disability or liability insurance is required by law or [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) rule, the applicant for the work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall obtain and include proof of such insurance with the work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) application. The [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall expire by operation of law if the insurance upon which the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) was conditioned lapses, expires or is cancelled, unless the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) holder files proof of alternate insurance before such event.

##### ***§28-105.12.7.1 Insurance Coverage for Adjacent Properties**

A person who obtains a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for construction or [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) operations shall, at such person's own expense, procure and maintain for the duration of the operations, insurance of a kind and in an amount specified by rule of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department), to insure any and all adjacent property [owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) and their lawful occupants fully for all risks of loss, damage to property or injury to or death of persons, arising out of or in connection with the performance of the proposed work. Such person shall submit proof of insurance to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) when applying for a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for construction or [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) work. The [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall provide such proof of such insurance together with the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) to the [owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of adjoining property thirty days prior to the commencement of the construction or [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) work, except in the event that emergency work is authorized as defined in [section 28-105.4.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-105.4.1) of this code. If such emergency work is necessary, the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) and proof of insurance shall be provided to [owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of adjoining property within a reasonable timeframe.

**Section 28-105.12.7.1 was amended by [New York State Laws of 2018 Chapter 217](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/nys_ch_217_adjoining_owner_notice.pdf). This law has an effective date of August 24, 2018.*

#### ***§28-105.12.8 Site Safety Plan**

Where a site safety plan is required by this code or by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department), all work shall adhere to the site safety plan. Site safety plans shall require approval of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) where specified in this code or the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014).

**Section 28-105.12.8 was amended by [Local Law 81 of 2017](http://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll81of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of November 6, 2017.*

#### ***§28-105.12.9 Safety Training Required**

No [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for construction or [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) work for which training is required by [section 3321](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/33/safeguards-during-construction-or-demolition#3321) of the New York city [building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014) shall be issued or renewed until the applicant has certified that all workers who will be working under such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) will have the requisite training throughout the duration of such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit).

**Section 28-105.12.9 was added by [Local Law 196 of 2017](http://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll196of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of October 16, 2017.*

#### ***§28-105.12.10 Tenant Protection Plan Required**

Where a [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan is required by [article 120](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#120), all work shall adhere to the [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan.

*Section 28-105.12.10 was added by [Local Law 106 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll106of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of March 8, 2020.

#### ***§28-105.12.11 Inspections**

Upon issuance of a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) and at any time during such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) period, the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) or his or her authorized representatives, in the discharge of their duties, shall have the right to enter, in accordance with applicable law, upon any buildings, enclosures, [premises](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#premises), or any part thereof, or attached thereto for the purposes of an inspection of work pursuant to such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) to ensure that such work is not occurring in an unsafe or dangerous manner, and that such work is being performed in compliance with applicable code provisions. If the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) or his or her authorized representative is unable to gain access to such property expeditiously for the purposes of an inspection of work pursuant to such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) and there is a reason to believe that the work is being done in violation of the law, the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall issue a stop work order. Such stop work order may be rescinded in accordance with [section 28-207.2.3](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/2/enforcement#§28-207.2.3).

**Section 28-105.12.11 was added by [Local Law 111 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll111of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of October 6, 2019.*

## **Article 106 Asbestos**

### **§28-106.1 Asbestos Certification Required**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall not issue a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for the [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) or [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) of a building constructed pursuant to plans submitted for approval on or before April 1, 1987, unless the applicant submits such certification relating to asbestos as may be required by the rules of the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of environmental protection.

#### ***§28-106.1.1 Full Demolition Permit**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall not issue a [full demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition_full) [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) unless the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of the building provides certification in a form and manner to be provided in the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of environmental protection that (i) the building is free of asbestos containing material, or (ii) the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) of environmental protection, has issued a variance from this requirement in accordance with subdivision (m) of section 24-136 of the administrative code and the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of environmental protection, subject to the requirement that [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) work will be performed only in parts of the building that are certified free of asbestos containing material. The [full demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition_full) [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be subject to such additional conditions as the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of buildings may require of the permittee based on the size and complexity of the [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) work.

**Exception:** This section 28-106.1.1 shall not apply to [full demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition_full) performed as emergency work pursuant to [article 215](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/2/enforcement#215) of [chapter 2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/2/enforcement#2) of this title where the emergency warrants immediate commencement of the work or [full demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition_full) with asbestos in place authorized pursuant to 12 NYCRR 56-11.5.

**Section 28-106.1.1 was amended by [Local Law 38 of 2015](http://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll38of2015.pdf). This law has an effective date of May 6, 2016.*

#### ***§28-106.1.2 Alteration Permit for the Removal of One or More Stories**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall not issue an [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for the removal of one or more stories of a building unless the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of the building provides certification in a form and manner to be provided in the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of environmental protection that (i) the stories to be removed are free of asbestos containing material and that no abatement activities will be performed anywhere in the building concurrently with the removal work authorized by such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) or (ii) the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) of environmental protection has issued a variance from these requirements in accordance with subdivision (m) of section 24-136 of the administrative code and the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of environmental protection, subject to the requirement that work authorized by the [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) will be performed only in parts of the building that are certified free of asbestos containing material. The [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be subject to such additional conditions as the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of buildings may require of the permittee based on the size and complexity of the work.


**Exception:** This section 28-106.1.2 shall not apply to removal of one or more stories performed as emergency work pursuant to [article 215](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/2/enforcement#215) of [chapter 2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/2/enforcement#2) of this title where the emergency warrants immediate commencement of the work.


**Section 28-106.1.2 was amended by [Local Law 38 of 2015](http://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll38of2015.pdf). This law has an effective date of May 6, 2016.*

### **§28-106.2 Construction and Maintenance of Asbestos Containment Structures and Other Temporary Structures or Work Required for Asbestos Abatement Activities**

Notwithstanding any other provision of this code, the construction and maintenance of asbestos containment structures, decontamination system enclosures and other temporary structures or work performed in the course of and only for the purpose of asbestos abatement activities shall comply with this section and the rules of the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of environmental protection relating to such temporary structures and work and with article 30 of the New York state labor law and rules adopted pursuant to such article.

#### **§28-106.2.1 Materials**
