The rules of the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of environmental protection relating to [materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials) used in the construction of temporary structures for asbestos abatement activities shall contain a provision requiring such structures to be non-combustible or flame resistant in compliance with reference standard NFPA 255-06 or NFPA 701-99, as such standards may be modified by local law or by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of buildings pursuant to applicable rules.

### **§28-106.3 Permit Exemption**

Except as otherwise provided by rule, work performed in the course of and only for the purpose of an asbestos [project](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#project) that is required to be permitted pursuant to section 24-138 of the administrative code shall be exempt from the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) requirements of this code.

**Section 28-106.3 was amended by [Local Law 38 of 2015](http://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll38of2015.pdf). This law has an effective date of May 6, 2016.*



### **§28-106.4 Definitions**

For the purposes of this article, the terms "asbestos" and "asbestos [project](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#project)" shall have the meanings as are ascribed in section 24-136 of the administrative code.

**Section 28-106.4 was amended by [Local Law 38 of 2015](http://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll38of2015.pdf). This law has an effective date of May 6, 2016.*



## **Article 107 Alteration or Demolition of Single Room Occupancy Multiple Dwellings**

### **§28-107.1 General**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall not approve [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents), nor issue an initial or reinstated [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) in connection therewith, for the [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) or [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) of a [single room occupancy multiple dwelling](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#single_room_occupancy_multiple_dwelling) except as set forth in this article. Applications for post approval amendments to [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) are subject to this article where the application proposes a change within a covered category of work as set forth in [section 28-107.3](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-107.3).

### **§28-107.2 Definitions**

The following words and terms shall, for the purposes of this article and elsewhere in the code, have the meanings shown herein.

**CLASS A MULTIPLE DWELLING, CLASS B MULTIPLE DWELLING, FURNISHED ROOM HOUSE, ROOMING UNIT AND SINGLE ROOM [OCCUPANCY](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy).** Shall have the meanings set forth in section 27-2004 of the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) housing maintenance code.

**[SINGLE ROOM OCCUPANCY MULTIPLE DWELLING](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#single_room_occupancy_multiple_dwelling).** A [single room occupancy multiple dwelling](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#single_room_occupancy_multiple_dwelling) means:

1. A "class A multiple dwelling" used in whole or part as a "rooming house" or "furnished room house," or for "single room [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy)" pursuant to section 248 of the [New York state multiple dwelling law](https://up.codes/viewer/ny-multiple-dwelling-law);
2. A "class A multiple dwelling" containing "rooming units"; or
3. A "class B multiple dwelling."


**Exception:** The term [single room occupancy multiple dwelling](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#single_room_occupancy_multiple_dwelling) shall not include:

1. College or school dormitories;

2. Clubhouses;

3. Luxury hotels, as such term is defined by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) of housing preservation and development; or

4. Residences whose [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) is restricted to an institutional use such as housing intended for use by the employees of a single company or institution;

5. [City](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city)-owned multiple dwellings; or

6. Any multiple dwelling, other than a lodging house, containing fewer than nine sleeping rooms, rooming units, single room [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) units, or hotel units unless the total number of such units is more than fifty percent of the total number of [dwelling units](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) in such multiple dwelling; or

7. Any multiple dwelling that:

   7.1 Is the subject of a program approved by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) of housing preservation and development and related to the rehabilitation or preservation of a [single room occupancy multiple dwelling](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#single_room_occupancy_multiple_dwelling) or the provision of housing for persons of low or moderate income, other than a program consisting solely of real property tax abatement or tax exemption; and

   7.2 Has been exempted from the provisions of this article by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) of housing preservation and development.





### **§28-107.3 Covered Categories of Work**

Applications for the approval of [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) for the following categories of work are covered by this article:

1. [Demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) of a [single room occupancy multiple dwelling](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#single_room_occupancy_multiple_dwelling);
2. [Alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) of a [single room occupancy multiple dwelling](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#single_room_occupancy_multiple_dwelling) to a class A multiple dwelling to be used in whole or in part for other than single room [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) purposes;
3. [Alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) of a [single room occupancy multiple dwelling](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#single_room_occupancy_multiple_dwelling) resulting in the removal or [addition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#addition) of kitchen or bathroom facilities; and
4. Such other types of [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) work to a [single room occupancy multiple dwelling](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#single_room_occupancy_multiple_dwelling) as shall be prescribed by rule of the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) of housing preservation and development, in consultation with the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner).

**Exceptions:**

1. Work solely for the purpose of either (i) making the public areas of a multiple dwelling accessible to persons with disabilities without altering the configuration of any [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) or rooming unit or (ii) making the interior or the entrance to a [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) or a rooming unit accessible to persons with disabilities shall not be covered by this article.
2. Repairs, [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) or any other work performed by a [city agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#city_agency) or by a contractor pursuant to a contract with a [city agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#city_agency) shall not be covered by this article.



### **§28-107.4 Required Submittal Documents**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall not approve any [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents), nor issue an initial or reinstated [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) in connection therewith, for a [single room occupancy multiple dwelling](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#single_room_occupancy_multiple_dwelling) for the covered categories of work unless the applicant provides:

1. A sworn affidavit by or on behalf of all the [owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner), as the term [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) is defined in section 27-2004 of the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) housing maintenance code, of such multiple dwelling that there will be no harassment of the lawful occupants of such multiple dwelling by or on behalf of such [owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) during the construction period;

2. A [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan as provided for in this code; and

3. One of the following documents from the commissioner of housing preservation and development:

   3.1 A current certification that there has been no harassment of the lawful occupants of such multiple dwelling within the 36 month period prior to submission of an application for such certification to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of housing preservation and development, provided, however, that such certification shall except any portion of such 36 month period during which title was vested in the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city); or

   3.2 A waiver of such certification.



### **§28-107.5 Filing Process**

Applications for a certification of no harassment shall be made pursuant to section 27-2093 of the housing maintenance code.

### **§28-107.6 Time Period for Acceptance or Rejection**

The time period in which the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) is required to approve or reject an application for construction document approval or resubmission thereof pursuant to this code shall commence from the date that the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) receives either the certification or waiver pursuant to this article.

### **§28-107.7 Denial of Certification**

Where the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) of housing preservation and development denies the certification required by this article, the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall reject the application for construction document approval.

### **§28-107.8 Request for Stop-Work or Rescission**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall be empowered to issue a stop-work notice or order with respect to an [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) or [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) and/or to rescind approval of [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) at the request of the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) of housing preservation and development pursuant to section 27-2093 of the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) housing maintenance code.

### **§28-107.9 Effect of Denial or Rescission**

Where the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) rejects or rescinds the approval of [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) pursuant to this article, no further application for the covered categories of work shall be considered by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) for a period of 36 months following the date of the denial of the certification of no harassment by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) of housing preservation and development or the date of the rescission of such certification of no harassment by such [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner).

## **Article 108 Pavement Plan**

### **§28-108.1 General**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall not issue a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for the erection of a new building or for [alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) that will require the issuance of a new or amended certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) without a statement that no certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) shall be issued unless the sidewalk in front of or abutting such building, including but not limited to the intersection quadrants for corner properties, shall have been paved or repaired by the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner), at his or her own cost, in the manner, of the [materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials), and in accordance with the standard specifications prescribed by the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of transportation pursuant to sections 19-113 and 19-115 of the administrative code.

**Exceptions:**

1. Application for the erection of an accessory building appurtenant to an existing one- or two-family dwelling.
2. Where the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) determines that a sidewalk is not required, provided that such determination shall not affect the obligations of the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) under subdivision a of section 19-152 of the administrative code, nor relieve the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of any such obligations, nor impair or diminish the rights of the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) or its agencies to enforce such obligations.
3. Where the extent of the change in use or [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) or the cost of the [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) does not exceed a threshold established pursuant to rule of the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner).



### **§28-108.2 Pavement Plan Required**

[Construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) shall include a pavement plan processed and approved under guidelines established by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). The pavement plan shall include documentation sufficient to show compliance with the standards and specifications of the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of transportation pursuant to sections 19-113 and 19-115 of the administrative code.

**Exception:** No pavement plan shall be required with respect to an [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) application for a building where the applicant certifies that there is a sidewalk in existence in front of or abutting such building, including but not limited to the intersection quadrants for corner properties, complying with the specifications of the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of transportation, and that the nature of such [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) work will neither remove such existing sidewalk nor cause damage to such existing sidewalk such that the damage could not be corrected as minor repairs prior to issuance of the certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy).

### **§28-108.3 Improvement of Streets**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall insure that streets are suitably improved in accordance with the standards and specifications of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of transportation as required by subdivision two of section thirty-six of the general [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) law and shall otherwise carry out the provisions of such subdivision.

## **Article 109 Fire Protection Plan**

### ***§28-109.1 Fire Protection Plan Required for Covered Buildings**

New building and [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) applications for [covered buildings](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#covered_building) as set forth in [section 28-109.2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-109.2) shall include a [fire protection plan](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#fire_protection_plan) prepared by or under the supervision of a registered design professional who shall professionally certify such plan. Such plan shall be submitted for review and approval by the fire [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) for compliance with this code prior to issuance of a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy), a temporary certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) or a [letter of completion](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#letter_of_completion), as applicable. The [fire protection plan](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#fire_protection_plan) shall be submitted in accordance with the rules and regulations of the fire [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department).


**Exception:** No [fire protection plan](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#fire_protection_plan) shall be required for an [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) that meets all three of the following requirements:

1. The [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) does not involve a change of use or [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy);
2. The [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) does not exceed one million dollars; and
3. The [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) does not create an inconsistency with a previously approved [fire protection plan](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#fire_protection_plan).


**Section 28-109.1 was amended by [Local Law 195 of 2018](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll195of2018.pdf). This law has an effective date of May 30, 2019.*

### **§28-109.2 Covered Buildings**

[Covered buildings](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#covered_building) include:

1. High-rise buildings as described in [section 403](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/4/special-detailed-requirements-based-on-use-and-occupancy#403) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014).
2. [Occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) groups B, E, F, H, M, or S occupying two or more stories with over 20,000 gross square feet (1858 m2) of floor area per floor, or occupying two or more stories in a building with a total floor area exceeding 50,000 gross square feet (4645 m2).
3. Any building containing an assembly [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) having an occupant load of 300 or more persons.
4. [Occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) group I or R- 1 occupying two or more stories and containing sleeping accommodations for 30 or more persons.
5. [Occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) group R-2 [occupancies](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) containing 30 or more [dwelling units](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) in a building where over 10,000 gross square feet (929 m2) of floor area is occupied by [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) group A, E, M, or I.
6. Covered mall buildings and open mall buildings designed pursuant to [section 402](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/4/special-detailed-requirements-based-on-use-and-occupancy#402) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014).



### **§28-109.3 Scope**

The plan shall include the following information, where applicable:

1. A description of the building including: address; block and lot numbers; number of stories; height in feet; [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) group; construction classification; [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) load and [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of buildings application number;

2. All floors, exits, doors, corridors, and partitions serving as fire barriers, fire partitions, fire walls; locations and ratings of required enclosures and fire areas; stairs with pressurization; roof access; exit discharges; and locations of any required frontage [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space); and

3. In narrative form, a description of safety systems and features, including:

   3.1 Communications systems.

   3.2 Alarm systems.

   3.3 Smoke and carbon monoxide detection equipment.

   3.4 Location of fire command station.

   3.5 Elevator recall.

   3.6 Emergency lighting and power.

   3.7 Standpipes.

   3.8 Sprinklers.

   3.9 Emergency and standby power systems.

   3.10 Mechanical ventilation and air conditioning.

   3.11 Smoke control systems and equipment.

   3.12 Furnishings types and [materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials).

   3.13 Places of assembly.

   3.14 Fire [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) access.

   3.15 Photoluminescent pathway markings.

   3.16 Other safety related systems, required and voluntary, to be installed.





## **Article 110 Site Safety Plan**

### **§28-110.1 Site Safety Plan**

Where a site safety plan is required by [chapter 33](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/33/safeguards-during-construction-or-demolition#33) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014), such plan shall include the following:

1. Location of all construction fences around work site;
2. Location of all gates in construction fences;
3. Location of standard guardrails around excavations, when required;
4. Horizontal and vertical netting program, including details of the initial installation, schedule of horizontal jumps and vertical installations, and designated crane and derrick lifting areas where horizontal netting is omitted. The program shall include as an attachment any [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) approval obtained regarding required safety netting during construction or [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) operations; the revised site safety plan shall be approved;
5. Location of all sidewalk sheds, including appropriate [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) application numbers and [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of transportation [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) numbers and expiration dates;
6. Location of all temporary walkways, including appropriate [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) application numbers and [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of transportation [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) numbers and expiration dates;
7. Location of foot bridges and motor vehicle ramps, including appropriate [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) application numbers and [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of transportation [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) numbers and expiration dates;
8. Protection of side of excavation, when required, including appropriate [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) application numbers and [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of transportation [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) numbers and expiration dates;
9. Location of all street and sidewalk closing(s), including appropriate [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) application numbers and [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of transportation [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) numbers and expiration dates;
10. Approximate location of material and personnel hoist(s) and loading areas, including appropriate [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) application numbers and [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of transportation [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) numbers and expiration dates;
11. Approximate location of all crane and derrick loading areas;
12. Location of all surrounding buildings, indicating [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy), height and type of any required roof protection;
13. Location of all standpipe system and siamese hose connections;
14. Location of all temporary elevators for fire [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) use when building is above 75 feet (22 860 mm) in height;
15. Location of all exterior contractors' sheds;
16. All required safety netting and scaffolding;
17. Widths of all sidewalks and roadways; all traffic information; all exits from the work site;
18. A copy of the proposed site safety manager or site safety coordinator's certificate, as applicable, including the certificate for any alternate site safety manager or site safety coordinator;
19. Such features requiring special sequencing in order to maintain safe conditions with a written description of those sequences;
20. A statement that prior to performing any work on the [project](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#project) all workers have successfully completed the training required by section 3310.10.2 of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014); and
21. A statement that all workers employed on the construction site will receive a site-specific orientation program required by [section 3310.10.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/33/safeguards-during-construction-or-demolition#*3310.10.1) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014).



### **§28-110.2 Phased Site Safety Plans**

Multiple layouts of the site safety features enumerated in [section 28-110.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-110.1) may be submitted at any time during construction operations to show phased site safety designs consistent with the phase of anticipated work.

## **Article 111 Temporary Structures and Uses**

### **§28-111.1 General**

The erection of certain temporary structures and temporary uses may be authorized as set forth in sections [28-111.1.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-111.1.1) and [28-111.1.2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-111.1.2).

#### **§28-111.1.1 Permits for the Erection and Use of Temporary Structures**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) is authorized to issue a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for the erection of temporary structures including but not limited to tents, grandstands, platforms, reviewing stands, outdoor bandstands, stages and similar miscellaneous structures and equipment, and for the temporary use of such structures. Such [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be limited as to time of service or use, but in no event shall be permitted for more than 90 days. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may grant extensions for demonstrated cause.

**Exception:** No [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be required for:

1. The erection and use of temporary tents of less than 400 gross square feet (37 m2) for not more than 30 days.
2. The erection and use of temporary platforms, reviewing stands, outdoor bandstands and similar miscellaneous structures that cover an area less than 120 square feet (11.16 m2), including connecting areas or [spaces](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space) with a common means of egress or entrance, for not more than 30 days.



#### **§28-111.1.2 Letters Authorizing Temporary Uses**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) is authorized to issue a letter authorizing the temporary use of outdoor or indoor [spaces](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space) provided the [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space) shall be occupied in a manner that will not endanger public safety, health, or welfare. Such letters authorizing the temporary use shall be limited as to time of service or use, but shall not be permitted for more than 90 days. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may grant extensions for demonstrated cause.

### **§28-111.2 Conformance**

Temporary structures and uses shall conform to the structural strength, fire safety, means of egress, accessibility, light, ventilation and sanitary requirements of this code as necessary to ensure the public health, safety and general welfare.

### **§28-111.3 Termination of Approval**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) is authorized to terminate such [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) or letter of authorization and to order the temporary structure or use to be discontinued.

### **§28-111.4 Application Processing**

Application for such structures and uses shall be submitted to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) no later than 15 business days prior to the construction of the temporary structure or the commencement of the temporary use.

### **§28-111.5 Fees**

Applications for such [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be accompanied by the applicable fees in accordance with [article 112](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#112). Fees for subsequent requests for renewals shall be paid upon approval of such requests.

### **§28-111.6 Place of Assembly**

Notwithstanding any inconsistent provision of this article the use of a temporary structure or the temporary use of [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space) as a place of assembly shall require a temporary place of assembly certificate of operation issued pursuant to [section 28-117.2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-117.2).

## **Article 112 Fees**

### **§28-112.1 Payment of Fees**

A [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit), inspection, or other service or privilege as regulated in this code shall not be valid until the fees prescribed herein or in rules have been paid, nor shall a renewal of a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) or other service or privilege or an amendment to a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) be released until the fee has been paid. In addition, an approval required to be reissued due to a change in product name, company name and/or address, contact information or principals, shall not be reissued until a reissuance fee, if any, has been paid. The [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall adopt such rules and shall prescribe such forms as may be necessary to carry out the provisions of this article.

**Exceptions:**

1. A [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit), inspection or other service or privilege as regulated in this code shall not be subject to this provision if the current deed holder of the building or property affected is a corporation or association organized and operated exclusively for religious, charitable or educational purposes, or for one or more such purposes, no part of the earnings of which inures to the benefit of any private shareholder or individual, and provided that the property affected is to be used exclusively by such corporation or association for one or more of such purposes.
2. A [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit), inspection or other service or privilege as regulated in this code shall not be subject to this provision if the work proposed is emergency work performed by a [city agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#city_agency) or by a contractor pursuant to a contract with a [city agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#city_agency).



### **§28-112.2 Schedule of Permit Fees**

[Permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for new buildings, structures, mechanical, and plumbing systems or [alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) requiring a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be accompanied by a fee for each [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) in accordance with the fee schedule of Table 28-112.2. Fifty percent of the total fee for the work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit), but not less than one hundred dollars, or the total fee for the work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) where such fee is less than one hundred dollars, shall be paid and shall accompany the first application for the approval of [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents); and the whole or remainder of the total fee shall be paid before the work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) may be issued. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may require reasonable substantiation of any statement or other form that may be required by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department).

| New Buildings                                                |                                                              |                                         |                                                              |
| New building work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit): One-, two- or three-family dwelling, where no existing building elements are to be retained in place as part of the new building.   Subsequent applications related to initial new building work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) application, filed prior to the first temporary certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) (TCO), or the final certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) if no TCO is issued. | $0.06 for each square foot, or fraction thereof, of the total floor area of the new building, but not less than $100 for each structure.                The rates and fees set forth above shall be subject to increases as provided by [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) rules.  $100 | $100                               $100 | For the purposes of this fee schedule item, "building elements" means any portion of an [existing building or structure](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#existing_building_or_structure), including but not limited to [party walls](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#party_wall) foundations, footings, piles and slabs on grade. |
| New building work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit): One-, two- or three-family dwelling, where any existing building elements are to be retained in place as part of the new building, pursuant to [section 28-101.4.5](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-101.4.5). | Minimum Filing Fee -$100             Minimum filing fee for the first five thousand dollars or fraction thereof, of the cost of [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration); plus $2.60 for each one thousand dollars, or fraction thereof, of cost of [alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) in excess of five thousand dollars.      The rates and fees set forth above shall be subject to increases as provided by [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) rules. | $100                                    | For the purposes of this fee schedule item, "building elements" means any portion of an [existing building or structure](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#existing_building_or_structure), including but not limited to [party walls](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#party_wall) foundations, footings, piles and slabs on grade. |
| New building work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit): Garage for not more than three cars when accessory to and filed with plans for one-, two- or three-family dwelling to which it is accessory on the same lot. | $100                                                         | $100                                    |                                                              |
| New building work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit): All other new buildings fewer than 7 stories and less than 100,000 square feet, where no existing building elements are to be retained in place as part of the new building.                                      Subsequent applications related to initial new building work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) application, filed prior to the first temporary certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) (TCO), or the final certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) if no TCO is issued. | $0.26 for each square foot, or fraction thereof, of the total floor area of the new building, but not less than $280 for each structure. | New building work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit): All other new buildings 7 stories or more or 100,000 square feet or more, classified in [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) group R-2, where at least 50 percent of the [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) units are affordable to households whose income is less than 165 percent of the area median income for New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city), as determined by the United States [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of housing and urban development or successor agency, which are financed entirely or in part by a grant or loan from the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) of New York or the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) housing and development corporation, and where no existing building elements are to be retained in place as part of the new building.                   Subsequent applications related to initial new building work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) application, filed prior to the first temporary certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) (TCO), or the final certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) if no TCO is issued. | $0.26 for each square foot, or fraction thereof, of the total floor area of the new building, but not less than $100 for each structure.              The rates and fees set forth above shall be subject to increases as provided by [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) rules.   $100 | $100                                    | For the purposes of this fee schedule item, "building elements" means any portion of an [existing building or structure](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#existing_building_or_structure), including but not limited to [party walls](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#party_wall) foundations, footings, piles and slabs on grade. |

**Table 28-112.2 was amended by [Local Law 56 of 2016](http://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll56of2016.pdf). This law has an effective date of June 9, 2016.*

### **§28-112.3 Building Permit Valuations**

An estimate of the cost of construction shall be provided at the time of application for construction document approval or, where no [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) are required, at the time of application for a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit). Such costs shall include the total value of work proposed, including but not limited to [materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials), equipment and labor, with reasonable allowances for profit and overhead. If, in the opinion of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department), the cost is underestimated, the application shall be denied, unless the applicant can show detailed estimates to meet the approval of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). A final affidavit with the total actual cost of construction, as built or installed, shall be submitted prior to signoff. The initial, amended and final building [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) valuation shall be set by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department).

### **§28-112.4 Work Commencing Before Permit Issuance**

Any person who commences any work before obtaining the necessary [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be subject to a penalty as specified in this code that shall be in addition to the required [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) fees.

### **§28-112.5 Related Fees**

The payment of the fee for the construction, [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration), removal or [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) for work done in connection or concurrently with the work authorized by a building [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall not relieve the applicant or holder of the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) from the payment of other fees that are prescribed by law.

### **§28-112.6 Refunds and Rebates**

Upon application to the comptroller of the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) of New York, and upon verification of claim by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner), refunds or rebates of partial or full fees shall be provided as set forth in sections [28-112.6.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-112.6.1) through [28-112.6.3](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-112.6.3).

#### **§28-112.6.1 Withdrawal of Work Permit Applications**

In the event that an [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) withdraws an application, the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) may obtain a refund of all or a portion of the fee paid as follows:

1. If an application for construction document approval is withdrawn prior to the commencement of examination of the application all but forty dollars of the deposit fee paid shall be refunded.
2. If an application for construction document approval is withdrawn during the progress of examination of the application, the comptroller shall retain a percentage of the deposit fee paid, which the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall certify is the equivalent percentage of the examination completed, but not less than one hundred dollars. The remainder of the deposit fee shall be refunded to the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner).
3. If an application for construction document approval is withdrawn after examination of [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and/or construction document approval and before issuance of [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit), there shall be refunded by the comptroller 50 percent of the total computed fee for the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit), except that not less than one hundred dollars shall be retained by the comptroller.



#### **§28-112.6.2 Withdrawal of Cranes and Derricks Applications**

If the applicant withdraws his or her application for a certificate of approval for a power-operated crane, derrick or cableway, such applicant may obtain a refund of a portion of the fees as follows:

1. If the application is withdrawn prior to the commencement of examination by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department), the entire fee shall be refunded except one hundred dollars.
2. If the application is withdrawn after the examination has commenced, the comptroller shall retain a percentage of the fee paid, which the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall certify is the equivalent percentage of the examination performed, but not less than one hundred dollars. The remainder of the fee shall be refunded to the applicant.
3. If the application is withdrawn after the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) has performed its examination, whether or not the application has been approved no part of the fee shall be returned to the applicant.



#### **§28-112.6.3 Incentive Rebates**

With respect to the rebates under this [section 28-112.6](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-112.6), the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may, at his or her discretion, issue a rebate of application fees as follows and as established by rule.

##### **§28-112.6.3.1 Renewable Energy Rebates**

[Owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) who demonstrate the production on a zoning lot of five percent or more of the annual [energy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#energy) consumption on the zoning lot through renewable [energy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#energy) sources may receive a fee rebate as established by rule.

##### **§28-112.6.3.2 Rebate for Energy Use Reduction**

[Owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) who demonstrate a reduction in [energy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#energy) use from that allowed at the time of [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) by the New York state [energy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#energy) conservation construction code as a result of the permitted work may receive a fee rebate as established by rule.

##### **§28-112.6.3.3 Rebate for Water Conservation Systems**

[Owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) who demonstrate conservation of water taken from the [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) supply by providing evidence of achieving the water-recycling discount authorized by the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) water board may receive a fee rebate as established by rule.

##### **§28-112.6.3.4 Rebate for Redevelopment, Remediation and Reuse of Contaminated Properties Known as Brownfields**

[Owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) who demonstrate that their site was contaminated and has been certified as remediated by the United States environmental protection agency or the New York state [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of environmental conservation, or has received a notice of satisfaction from the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of environmental protection, may receive a fee rebate as established by rule.

##### **§28-112.6.3.5 Rebate for Recycling Construction and Demolition Waste**

[Owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) who demonstrate the recycling of construction and [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) waste may receive a fee rebate as established by rule.

##### **§28-112.6.3.6 Rebate for Bicycle Storage Facilities**

Except for R-3 [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy), [owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) who demonstrate that they have provided secured indoor bicycling facilities accessible to all building occupants may be rebated their fees as set out in rule. Such facilities shall be identified on approved plans and shall be noted on the certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) with a statement that the bicycling accommodations dedicated to such facilities were provided in accordance with this section.

##### **§28-112.6.3.7 Rebate for LEED or Other Environmental Design Certification**

[Owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) who demonstrate certification of their [project](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#project), which was signed off following the effective date of this code, by the United States Green Building Council based upon the Council's Leadership in [Energy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#energy) and Environmental Design (LEED) rating system or as otherwise provided by rule, may be rebated their fees as set out in rule.

##### **§28-112.6.3.8 Other Rebates**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) is authorized to promulgate rules to rebate fees following [sign-off](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#sign-off) based upon the installation of [energy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#energy)-conserving systems.

### **§28-112.7 Inspection and Report Filing Fees**

Aside from the fees covered under [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) fees above, the following inspection and report filing fees shall be paid according to requirements of this code and as promulgated in rules.

#### **§28-112.7.1 Fees for the Testing, Approval, Inspection and Use of Power-Operated Cranes, Derricks and Cableways**

The [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of any crane or derrick shall renew the certificate of operation each year. See [Table 28-112.7.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#table_28-112.7.1).

### **§28-112.9 Lien on Premises for Unpaid Fee or Other Charge**

Any unpaid fee or charge for an inspection, reinspection, examination or service performed by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) or other unpaid amount owed to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department), and all [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) issued by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department), pursuant to law shall constitute a lien upon the land and buildings upon or in respect to which such inspection, reinspection, examination or service was performed or [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) issued, as hereinafter provided.

### **§28-112.9.1 Filing of Fees**

The [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall maintain a record of all unpaid fees and other charges. Such records shall be kept on a building by building basis and shall be accessible to the public during business hours. An entry of an unpaid amount on the records of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall constitute notice to all parties.

#### **§28-112.9.2 Lien**

All such unpaid amounts shall constitute a lien upon the land and building upon, or in respect to which, such inspection, reinspection, examination or service was performed or [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) issued when the amount thereof shall have been definitely computed as a statement of account by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) and the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall file such statement with the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of finance for entry in the records of such [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) against the [premises](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#premises). Such lien shall have a priority over all other liens and encumbrances except for the lien of taxes and assessments. However, no lien created pursuant to this [section 28-112.9](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-112.9) shall be enforced against a subsequent purchaser in good faith or mortgagee in good faith unless the requirements of [section 28-112.9.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-112.9.1) are satisfied.

#### **§28-112.9.3 Notice**

A notice, stating the amount due and the nature of the charge, shall be mailed by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of finance, to the last known address of the person whose name appears on the records in the office of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of finance as being the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) or agent or as the person designated by the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) to receive tax bills or, where no name appears, to the [premises](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#premises), addressed to either the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) or the agent.

#### **§28-112.9.4 Interest**

If such charge is not paid within 30 days from the date of entry, it shall be the duty of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of finance to receive interest thereon at the rate of 15 percent per annum, to be calculated to the date of payment from the date of entry.

#### **§28-112.9.5 Tax Lien**

Such charge and the interest thereon shall continue to be, until paid, a lien on the [premises](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#premises). Such lien shall be deemed a tax lien within the meaning of sections 11-319 and 11-401 of the administrative code and may be sold, enforced or foreclosed in the manner provided in chapter three or four of title eleven of such code or may be satisfied in accordance with the provisions of section thirteen hundred fifty-four of the real property actions and proceedings law.

#### **§28-112.9.6 Reference**

The notice mailed by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of finance pursuant to this [section 28-112.9](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-112.9) shall have stamped or printed thereon a reference to this [section 28-112.9](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-112.9).

#### **§28-112.9.7 Validity Not Subject to Challenge in Enforcement Proceeding**

In any proceedings to enforce or discharge a lien created pursuant to this [section 28-112.9](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-112.9) the validity of the lien shall not be subject to challenge based on:

1. The lawfulness of the inspection, reinspection, examination, service or [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit); or
2. The propriety and accuracy of the fee for which a lien is claimed, except as provided in this [section 28-112.9](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-112.9).



#### **§28-112.9.8 Standing to Challenge**

No such challenge may be made except by (i) the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of the property, or (ii) a mortgagee or lienor whose mortgage or lien would, but for the provisions of this [section 28-112.9](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-112.9), have priority over the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department)'s lien.

### **§28-112.10 Waiver of Application, Permit and Inspection Fees for Certain Work Arising Out of the Storm That Occurred on October 29 and 30, 2012**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall waive the fees that would otherwise be required to be paid by this code, the [electrical code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-electrical-code-2011) or the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) for applications, [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) and inspections for certain work arising out of the storm that occurred on October 29 and 30, 2012 as provided in subsections [28-112.10.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-112.10.1) and [28-112.10.2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-112.10.2).

#### **§28-112.10.1 Eligible Buildings**
