For the purposes of this article, eligible buildings that, following the storm and pursuant to an inspection program established by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) under an emergency order of the Mayor, are designated by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) after inspection through a notation on the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department)'s records and/or by the posting of a red placard warning on the building or [premises](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#premises) as seriously damaged and unsafe to enter or occupy or completely demolished and/or washed away. With respect to eligible buildings, fees associated with applications, [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) and inspections shall be waived for [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) work, [demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition) work, construction of new buildings and associated work, including but not limited to associated electrical and [plumbing work](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#plumbing_work). The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may request the applicant to submit additional information relating to the damage. Waiver of such fees pursuant to this section shall be applicable for jobs where the initial application for construction document approval or, if no [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) are required, application for [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is submitted on or after October 30, 2012 and on or before October 31, 2014.

#### **§28-112.10.2 Storm Related Damage to Electrical and Plumbing Systems**

In buildings other than eligible buildings, fees shall be waived only for applications, [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) and inspections for work related to plumbing and electrical systems damaged by such storm. Applicants must submit certification by a licensed master electrician or a licensed master plumber or fire suppression piping contractor that the proposed work is related to such storm damage. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may request the applicant to submit additional information relating to the damage. Waiver of such fees pursuant to this section shall be applicable for jobs where the initial application for construction document approval or, if no [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) are required, application for [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is submitted on or after October 30, 2012 and on or before December 31, 2013.

### **§28-112.11 Waiver of Application, Permit and Inspection Fees for Work Funded Under the "Build It Back" Program**

The [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) has implemented a disaster recovery program known as the Build It Back program that uses federal Community Development Block Grant Disaster Recovery funds to aid in the recovery of residential property damaged or destroyed in the severe storm known as Sandy that occurred on October 29 and 30, 2012. To assist in such recovery, the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall waive fees, which would otherwise be required to be paid to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) by this code, the [electrical code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-electrical-code-2011) or the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department), in connection with applications, [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) and inspections for work that is officially approved and funded under the Build It Back program. The waiver provided for in this section shall apply only to work performed on property that is classified as residential and to fees payable on or after July 1, 2014. With respect to work on a mixed use building, fees payable on or after such date may only be waived for work on the residential units of such building and portions of such building that serve the residential units.

### ***§28-112.12 Reduction in Fees or Penalties for Sponsoring Site Safety Training**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall establish by rule a program for reducing the amount of any fee to be imposed upon a person or any civil penalty to be imposed upon a person for a violation, other than an immediately hazardous violation, where one or more of the following conditions is satisfied:

1. Such person demonstrates, in a form and manner established by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner), that such person has paid, either directly or indirectly, for the costs of one or more workers to obtain the training needed to comply with section 3321 of the New York city building code or has otherwise arranged for such workers to receive such training at no cost to such workers, provided that this shall not include any worker trained pursuant to an agreement that such person was required to enter into pursuant to [section 28-204.1.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/2/enforcement#*§28-204.1.1) or any worker trained under a program developed pursuant to section 22-509.
2. The fee or penalty to be imposed upon such person related to a building site for which the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of such site, or a person acting on such [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner)'s behalf, demonstrates, in a form and manner established by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner), that such [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) or such person acting on such [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner)'s behalf has paid, either directly or indirectly, for the costs of one or more workers to obtain the training needed to comply with [section 3321](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/33/safeguards-during-construction-or-demolition#3321) of the New York city [building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014) or has otherwise arranged for such workers to receive such training at no cost to such workers, provided that this shall not include any worker trained pursuant to an agreement such person was required to enter into pursuant to [section 28-204.1.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/2/enforcement#*§28-204.1.1) or any worker trained under a program developed pursuant to section 22-509.

**Section 28-112.12 was added by [Local Law 196 of 2017](http://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll196of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of October 16, 2017.*

## **Article 113 Materials**

### **§28-113.1 General**

[Materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials) shall be used, tested and approved for use in accordance with the specific provisions of this code and [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) rules, except that the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall have the power to limit or prohibit the use of any material to protect public safety. [Materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials) shall be identified or described on [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and other related documents.

### **§28-113.2 Use of Materials**

Except as set forth in sections [28-113.2.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-113.2.1) through [113.2.6](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-113.2.6) [materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials) specifically prescribed by this code or [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) rules may be used as prescribed without the prior approval of the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner).

#### **§28-113.2.1 Approved Material**

Whenever this code or the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) requires the use of an approved material, such material shall not be used without the prior approval of the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) for such use and may be used only to the extent set forth in such approval.

#### **§28-113.2.2 Alternative Materials**

Except as otherwise specifically limited by this code, the provisions of this code are not intended to prevent the installation of any material or to prohibit any alternative engineered design or method of construction not specifically prescribed by this code, provided that the use of such alternative material has been previously approved by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) and may be used only to the extent set forth in such approval. The use of an alternative material, design, method of construction or equipment shall be approved where the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) finds that the proposed design is satisfactory and complies with the intent of the provisions of this code, and that the material, method or work offered is, for the purpose intended, at least the equivalent of that prescribed in this code in quality, strength, effectiveness, fire resistance, durability and safety.

#### **§28-113.2.3 Listed or Labeled**

Whenever this code or the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) requires that material used be listed or [labeled](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#labeled) to a standard, material that is so listed or [labeled](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#labeled) may be used in accordance with such list or [label](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#label) without the prior approval of the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner). However, the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) reserves the right to require that information be submitted with regard to the testing and evaluation of any material so listed or [labeled](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#labeled) including but not limited to [inspection certificates](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#inspection_certificate), test or evaluation reports, analysis, computations or other information used to determine that the material so listed or [labeled](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#labeled) complies with the applicable standard.

#### **§28-113.2.4 Material Not Listed or Labeled**

Whenever this code or the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) requires that material be listed or [labeled](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#labeled) to a standard and material proposed to be used is not so listed or [labeled](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#labeled), the use of such material shall be subject to prior approval by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) and such material shall be used only to the extent set forth in such approval.

#### **§28-113.2.5 Reuse**

The use of used material that meets the requirements of this code for new material is permitted unless otherwise provided in this code. Used equipment and devices shall not be reused without the prior approval of the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) and may be used only to the extent set forth in such approval.

#### **§28-113.2.6 Previously Issued Approvals**

[Materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials) that were previously approved by the board of standards and appeals or by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) before July [1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#1), 2008 may continue to be used to the extent that such approval is not inconsistent with the requirements or standards of this code, unless specifically amended or repealed by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner).

### **§28-113.3 Approval Procedure**

Approval of [materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials) pursuant to [section 28-113.2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-113.2) shall be in accordance with procedures set forth in this code and the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). The cost offsets, reports and investigations required under these provisions shall be paid by the applicant.

#### **§28-113.3.1 Performance**

When required by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner), specific information consisting of test reports conducted by an [approved testing agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_testing_agency) in accordance with standards referenced in the construction codes or other such information as necessary, shall be provided for the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) to determine whether the material will perform for the use intended.

#### **§28-113.3.2 Research and Investigation**

When required by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner), sufficient technical data shall be submitted to the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) to substantiate the proposed use of any material. If it is determined that the evidence submitted is satisfactory proof of performance for the use intended, the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall approve the use of the material subject to the requirements of this code.

#### **§28-113.3.3 Retesting of Materials**

All [materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials) tested and accepted for use shall be subject to periodic retesting as determined by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner); and any material that upon retesting is found not to comply with the code requirements or the requirements set forth in the approval of such material shall cease to be acceptable for the use intended. During the period for such retesting, the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may require the use of such material to be restricted or discontinued if necessary to secure safety.

#### **§28-113.3.4 New Materials**

New [materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials) not provided for in this code, and any material of questioned suitability proposed for use in the construction of a building or structure, shall be subjected to the tests prescribed in this code or in the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) to determine character, quality and limitations of use.

#### **§28-113.3.5 Research Reports**

Supporting data, where necessary to assist in the approval of [materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials) not specifically provided for in this code, shall consist of valid research reports from approved sources or other equivalent approved supporting documentation.

#### **§28-113.3.6 Conflicting Test Results**

Whenever there is evidence of conflicting results in the test of any material, the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall determine the acceptability of the material and/or the acceptable rating for such material.

#### **§28-113.3.7 Amendment and Repeal**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall have the power to amend or repeal the approval of any material, including [materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials) previously approved by the board of standards and appeals.

#### **§28-113.3.8 Maintenance of Records of Approved Material**

For any material that has been approved, a record of such approval, including the conditions and limitations of the approval, shall be posted on the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department)'s website or shall be made available for public inspection at appropriate times.

### **§28-113.4 Labeling**

[Materials](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#materials) required to be [labeled](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#labeled) shall be [labeled](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#labeled) in accordance with the procedures set forth in this code or the recognized referenced standards.

#### **§28-113.4.1 Testing**

An [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall test a representative sample of the material being [labeled](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#labeled) to the relevant standard or standards. The [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall maintain a record of the tests performed. The record shall provide sufficient detail to verify compliance with the test standard.

#### **§28-113.4.2 Inspection and Identification**

The [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall at regular intervals perform surveillance inspections, which shall be in-plant if necessary, of the material that is to be [labeled](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#labeled). The inspection shall verify that the [labeled](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#labeled) material is representative of the material tested.

#### **§28-113.4.3 Label Information**

The [label](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#label) shall contain the manufacturer's or distributor's identification, model number, serial number or definitive information describing the material's performance characteristics and the [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency)'s identification.

#### **§28-113.4.4 Shipment and Delivery Certification of Materials Listed, Labeled or Approved**

In the case of the shipment or delivery of material listed or [labeled](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#labeled) to a standard, such material shall be appropriately [labeled](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#labeled) or accompanied by the [inspection certificate](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#inspection_certificate) of an [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) that the material is the same as that which was tested and evaluated by such agency. In the case of the shipment or delivery of material previously approved by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner), the material shall be identified by a tag or certificate indicating that the material is the same that was approved for its intended use by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) or, if applicable, previously approved by the board of standards and appeals, and containing the applicable approval number or calendar number under which the material received such approval.

### **§28-113.5 Volatile Organic Compounds Emissions in Carpet and Carpet Cushion**

On and after July 1, 2013 carpet and carpet cushion as defined in section 17-1401 of the administrative code shall comply with the limits on volatile organic compound emissions set forth in chapter 14 of title 17 of such code.

## **Article 114 Approved Agencies**

### **§28-114.1 General**

[Approved agencies](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall satisfy the provisions of this article and the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) as to qualifications and operations. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may revoke or suspend the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner)'s approval of or otherwise sanction an [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) for cause.

#### **§28-114.1.1 Independent**

An [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall perform its authorized duties objectively and competently. The agency shall disclose possible conflicts of interest so that objectivity can be confirmed.

#### **§28-114.1.2 Testing Equipment**

An [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall have adequate testing equipment to perform required tests. The equipment shall be periodically calibrated.

#### **§28-114.1.3 Personnel**

An [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall employ experienced personnel qualified to conduct, supervise and evaluate the tests or inspections that it undertakes. [Special inspections](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection) may be performed only by employees of such agency who are [special inspectors](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspector) qualified pursuant to [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) rules to perform or witness the particular test or inspection. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may require proof of the qualifications of employees.

#### **§28-114.1.4 Background**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may require an [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) to submit to an investigation of its background and of the background of its principals as a condition of approval.

#### **§28-114.1.5 Insurance**

An [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall maintain liability insurance as required by [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) rules.

### **§28-114.2 Written Evaluation by Approved Agency**

An agency's evaluation of material or report of an inspection shall be in [writing](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#writing) after satisfactory completion of the required inspection or test.

### **§28-114.3 Records**

The [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall maintain records of inspection and test reports for at least six years or for such period as the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall determine and shall make such records available to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) upon request.

### **§28-114.4 RE-Authorization of Approved Agencies**

An [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall have its approval re-authorized in accordance with rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department).

## **Article 115 Special Inspection Agencies and Special Inspectors**

### **§28-115.1 General**

[Special inspection agencies](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection_agency) are [approved agencies](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) and shall be subject to the provisions of [article 114](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#114) of this chapter. [Special inspection agencies](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection_agency) and [special inspectors](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspector) shall satisfy the provisions of this article and the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) as to qualifications in order to perform [special inspections](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection) required by [chapter 17](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/17/structural-tests-and-special-inspections#17) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014) or elsewhere in this code or [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) rules.

### **§28-115.2 Disqualification**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may disqualify a [special inspection agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection_agency) or a [special inspector](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspector) from performing [special inspections](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection) pursuant to this code for cause. The [special inspection agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection_agency) or [special inspector](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspector) shall be given prior notice of the proposed disqualification and the opportunity to contest such action. A list of [special inspection agencies](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection_agency) and [special inspectors](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspector) who have been disqualified from performing [special inspection](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection) shall be maintained and made available to the public upon request.

### **§28-115.3 Records**

A [special inspector](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspector) shall maintain records of [special inspections](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection) on a building by building basis for at least 6 years or for such period as the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall determine and shall make such records available to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) upon request.

## **Article 116 Inspections and Sign-Off of Completed Work**

### **§28-116.1 General**

Construction or work for which a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is required shall be subject to inspection in accordance with this code and such construction or work shall remain accessible and exposed for inspection purposes until the required inspection is completed. A satisfactory inspection by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) or the acceptance by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of a satisfactory report of an inspection by an [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall not be construed to be an approval by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of a violation of the provisions of this code or of any other provision of law. It shall be the duty of the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) holder to cause the work to remain accessible and exposed for inspection purposes. The [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) holder shall be liable for any expense entailed in the removal or replacement of any material required to allow inspection. The inspector shall supply a report of the results of each inspection.

#### **§28-116.1.1 Defective Work and Discrepancies With Approved Construction Documents**

An [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) conducting inspections shall report defective work and discrepancies with the approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) to the contractor and, when applicable, to the [superintendent of construction](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#superintendent_of_construction), for correction. The [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall report uncorrected discrepancies and defective work to the [registered design professional of record](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#registered_design_professional_of_record) and the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) in [writing](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#writing).

#### **§28-116.1.2 Hazardous Conditions**

The [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall report all conditions noted as hazardous to life, safety or health that are not immediately corrected to the immediate attention of the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner).

### **§28-116.2 Types of Inspections**

The inspections set forth in sections [28-116.2.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#*§28-116.2.1) through [28-116.2.4](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#*§28-116.2.4) are required or authorized by this code.

#### ***§28-116.2.1 Preliminary Inspection**

Before approving [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents), the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) is authorized to examine or cause to be examined structures or [premises](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#premises) for which an application has been filed. The [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall conduct preliminary inspections of no less than 20 percent of buildings containing six or more units where (i) an application for [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) is submitted to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) and (ii) the applicant has indicated that the building that is the subject of such application is unoccupied, in order to verify the [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) status of such sites.

**Section 28-116.2.1 was amended by [Local Law 115 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll115of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of January 1, 2020.*

##### ***§28-116.2.1.1 Preliminary Inspection Reporting**

By January 1, 2021 and no later than January 1 annually thereafter, the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of buildings shall submit to the mayor and the speaker of the council a report describing the findings of preliminary inspections performed pursuant to [section 28-116.2.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#*§28-116.2.1) in the preceding year. Such report shall include, but not be limited to: (i) the total number of applications found to have falsely indicated that a building was unoccupied; and (ii) for each application found to have falsely indicated that a building was unoccupied, the location of the associated building and date of filing for such application.

**Section 28-116.2.1.1 was added by [Local Law 115 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll115of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of January 1, 2020.*

#### **§28-116.2.2 Compliance Inspections**

In addition to the inspections specified in this code, the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) is authorized to make or require other inspections of any construction work to ascertain compliance with the provisions of this code and other laws that are enforced by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department).

#### **§28-116.2.3 Special Inspections, Progress Inspections and Other Inspections Required During the Progress of Work**

After the issuance of a work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit), [special inspections](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection), [progress inspections](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#progress_inspection) and other inspections required by this code to be made during the progress of the work shall be made at such times or at such stages of the work and in such manner as shall be provided by this code or as otherwise required by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner). The [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) application shall set forth an inspection program for the work. Such inspections may be made by [approved agencies](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) or by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) as provided in this code or in the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). [Special inspections](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection) shall be performed only by individuals who are [special inspectors](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspector). The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may accept inspection and test reports from [approved agencies](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) and the work may, unless otherwise specifically provided by code provisions or directed by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner), proceed without any verifying inspection or test by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). The names and business addresses of [special inspectors](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspector) and [approved agencies](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall be set forth in the work [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) application. All inspection reports shall be in [writing](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#writing) and signed by the person or entity performing the inspection. A record of all inspections shall be kept by the person performing the inspection. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may require inspection reports to be filed with the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). Records of inspections made by [approved agencies](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) and [special inspectors](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspector) shall be maintained by such persons for a period of six years after [sign-off](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#sign-off) of the work or for such other period of time as the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may require and shall be made available to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) upon request.

##### **§28-116.2.3.1 Special and Progress Inspection of Fabricated Items**

Where fabrication of regulated products is performed on the [premises](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#premises) of a fabricator's shop, special or [progress inspection](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#progress_inspection) of the [fabricated items](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#fabricated_item) is required. The [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall verify that the fabricator maintains detailed fabrication and quality control procedures that provide a basis for inspection control of the workmanship and the fabricator's ability to conform to approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and referenced standards. The [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall review the procedures for completeness and adequacy relative to the code requirements for the fabrica-tor's scope of work.
Exception:

1. Work that is subject to [progress inspections](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#progress_inspection) and performed on the fabricator's [premises](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#premises) shall not be subject to [progress inspections](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#progress_inspection) where the fabricator is approved by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) in accordance with [section 28-116.6](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-116.6).
2. Work that is subject to [special inspections](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection) and performed on the fabricator's [premises](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#premises) shall be inspected by the [special inspection agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection_agency) in accordance with [Section 1704.2.2.3](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/17/structural-tests-and-special-inspections#1704.2.2.3) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014) where the fabricator is approved by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) in accordance with [section 28-116.6](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-116.6).



##### **§28-116.2.3.2 Special Inspection of Raising and Moving of a Building**

Where the lowest above-grade floor or the lowest subgrade floor of a building is to be raised, lifted, elevated or moved, [special inspection](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection) of such work is required. The [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) holder shall notify the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) in [writing](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#writing) at least 48 hours before the commencement of such work.

#### ***§28-116.2.4 Final Inspection**

There shall be a final inspection of all permitted work. Final inspections shall comply with sections [28-116.2.4.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-116.2.4.1) through [28-116.2.4.3](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#*§28-116.2.4.3).

**Section 28-116.2.4 was amended by [Local Law 151 of 2016](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll151of2016.pdf). This law has an effective date of January 1, 2018.*

##### **§28-116.2.4.1 Final Inspection Prior to Certificate of Occupancy**

In all cases where the permitted work requires the issuance of a new or amended certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy), the final inspection shall be performed by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) in the presence of the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) holder, the [registered design professional of record](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#registered_design_professional_of_record) or the [superintendent of construction](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#superintendent_of_construction). Such inspection shall be performed after all work authorized by the building [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is completed and before the issuance of the certificate of occupancy. All failures to comply with the provisions of this code or approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) shall be noted and the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) promptly notified thereof in [writing](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#writing). All defects noted in such inspection shall be corrected. Reports of such final inspections shall be maintained by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). The final inspection report shall confirm that defects noted have been corrected, that the work is in substantial compliance with the approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and with this code and with other applicable laws and rules and that all required inspections were performed.
Exception: For amended certificates of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) subject to [section 28-118.16.2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-118.16.2), the term [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents), as used in section 28-116.2.4.1, shall consist of an accurate and complete final lot survey made by a [land surveyor](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#land_surveyor), and floor and roof plans showing, at a minimum, compliance with exit requirements in accordance with this code.

##### ***§28-116.2.4.2 Final Inspection Prior to Letter of Completion**

In all cases where the permitted work does not require the issuance of a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy), the final inspection shall be performed by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) or at the option of the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) by an [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency). Whenever the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) performs a final inspection, the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall charge a fee for such inspection. The applicant shall take all reasonable and necessary steps to ensure that the final inspection is performed within one year after the expiration of the last [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit). The inspection shall be performed after all work authorized by the building [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is completed. The [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) performing the inspection shall report defective work and discrepancies with the approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) to the contractor and, when applicable, to the [superintendent of construction](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#superintendent_of_construction), for correction. The [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall report uncorrected discrepancies and defective work to the [registered design professional of record](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#registered_design_professional_of_record) and the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) in [writing](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#writing). The [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall report all conditions noted or observed as hazardous to life, safety or health that are not immediately corrected to the immediate attention of the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner). All defects noted in such inspection shall be corrected. The final inspection report shall confirm that defects noted have been corrected, that the work is in substantial compliance with the approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and with this code and other applicable laws and rules and that all required inspections were performed. Final inspection reports shall be filed with and maintained by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). Records of final inspections made by [approved agencies](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency) shall be maintained by such persons for a period of six years after [sign-off](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#sign-off) or for such other period as the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall require and shall be made available to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) upon request.
Exception: Final inspection shall be performed by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) for permitted work in R-2 [occupancies](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) if the building is listed on the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of housing preservation and development's website pursuant to paragraph 6 of subdivision m of section 27-2115.

**Section 28-116.2.4.2 was amended by [Local Law 149 of 2017](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll149of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of December 28, 2017.*

##### ***§28-116.2.4.3 Final Inspection of Gas Piping Systems**

The final inspection of gas piping systems shall be performed by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) in the presence of the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) holder, the [registered design professional of record](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#registered_design_professional_of_record) or the [superintendent of construction](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#superintendent_of_construction). Such inspection shall be performed after all work authorized by the building [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) is completed. All failures to comply with the provisions of this code or approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) shall be noted and the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) promptly notified thereof in [writing](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#writing). All defects noted in such inspection shall be corrected. Reports of such final inspections shall be maintained by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). The final inspection report shall confirm that defects noted have been corrected, that the work is in substantial compliance with the approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and with this code and with other applicable laws and rules and that all required inspections were performed.

**Section 28-116.2.4.3 was added by [Local Law 151 of 2016](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll151of2016.pdf). This law has an effective date of January 1, 2018.*

### **§28-116.3 Inspection Requests**

It shall be the duty of the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) holder to notify the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) or the person or entity designated to perform the inspection when work requiring inspection is ready to be inspected. It shall be the duty of the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) holder to provide access to and means for inspection of such work for any inspections that are required by this code.

#### **§28-116.3.1 Additional Notifications for Special Inspections**

The [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) holder shall also notify the relevant [special inspection agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection_agency) in [writing](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#writing) at least 72 hours prior to the commencement of any work requiring [special inspection](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#special_inspection).

### **§28-116.4 Sign-Off of Completed Work**

Upon submission of a satisfactory report of final inspection and all required [submittal documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#submittal_documents), the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall document the [sign-off](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#sign-off) of the [project](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#project) and issue a [letter of completion](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#letter_of_completion), or, if applicable, a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) for the work. The [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) shall take all necessary steps required by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) for the issuance of such [letter of completion](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#letter_of_completion) or certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) within 1 year following the expiration of the last [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit).

#### **§28-116.4.1 Issuance of Certificate of Compliance**

The following types of [service equipment](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#service_equipment) shall not be operated until the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) issues a [certificate of compliance](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#certificate_of_compliance) after submission of a satisfactory report of inspection and testing of such equipment in accordance with this code and all required [submittal documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#submittal_documents):

1. Air-conditioning, ventilation and exhaust systems.
2. Elevators, escalators, moving walkways and dumbwaiters.
3. Fuel burning and fuel-oil storage equipment.
4. Refrigeration systems.
5. Heating systems.
6. Boilers.

**Exception:** A [certificate of compliance](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#certificate_of_compliance) shall not be required in connection with work specifically exempted from [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) requirements in accordance with this code or [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) rules.

### **§28-116.5 Payment of Outstanding Penalties**

The [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) may refuse to issue a [letter of completion](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#letter_of_completion) or certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) pending payment of all outstanding fines or civil penalties imposed for violations of this code, the [1968 building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-1968-v1) or other laws enforced by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) at the same building.

### **§28-116.6 Fabricator Approval**

Approval of fabricators by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall be based upon review of the fabricator's written procedural and quality control manuals and periodic auditing of fabrication practices by an [approved agency](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_agency).

#### **§28-116.6.1 Fabricator's Certificate of Compliance**

For all [fabricated items](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#fabricated_item), the [approved fabricator](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#approved_fabricator) shall submit a [certificate of compliance](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#certificate_of_compliance) to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) stating that the work was performed in accordance with the approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents), referenced standards and applicable provisions of law.

## **Article 117 Places of Assembly**

### **§28-117.1 Place of Assembly Certificate of Operation**

It shall be unlawful to use or occupy any building or [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space), including an outdoor [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space), as a place of assembly without a certificate of operation issued by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner). An application for a certificate of operation shall be made to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) in such form and containing such information as the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall provide. The [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall inspect every place of assembly [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space) prior to the issuance of a certificate of operation. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall not issue a certificate of operation unless the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) determines that the [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space) conforms substantially to the approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and to this code or the [1968 building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-1968-v1) as applicable and that the certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) authorizes such use. A certificate of operation shall not be issued to a place of assembly providing seating or other moveable furnishings unless the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) approves a plan conforming to this code or the [1968 building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-1968-v1) as applicable and the rules of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). Seating and other moveable furnishings shall be maintained at all times during [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) in accordance with the approved plan. Any amendment of such plan shall be subject to the prior approval of the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner).

**§28-117.1.1 Contents of the Place of Assembly Certificate of Operation**

The certificate of operation shall contain the place of assembly certificate number, the number of persons who may legally occupy the [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space) and any other information that the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may determine. Such certificate of operation shall be framed and mounted in a location that is conspicuously visible to a person entering the [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space). For the purposes of this article a [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) issued place of assembly [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) or place of assembly certificate of operation shall be valid until its expiration, at which time a new place of assembly certificate of operation shall be required in accordance with the provisions of this article and with the filing requirements of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department).

#### **§28-117.1.2 New Certificate Required**

The following changes to a place of assembly shall require a new place of assembly certificate of operation instead of an amendment filed in accordance with [section 28-117.1.3](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-117.1.3):

1. For a [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) issued place of assembly [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) or place of assembly certificate of operation that does not have a nine-digit job number, any change of zoning use group, assembly [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) group A-1 through A-5, or any of the changes set forth in [section 28-117.1.3](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-117.1.3).
2. For all other [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) issued place of assembly [permits](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) or place of assembly certificates of operation, any change of zoning use group or assembly [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) group A-1 through A-5.



#### **§28-117.1.3 Amendments**

No change shall be made to a place of assembly that is inconsistent with the most recently issued place of assembly certificate of operation or renewal unless an amendment to such certificate is filed with and approved or accepted by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). Changes that require an amendment include any of the following:

1. Any physical change requiring an [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) to be issued by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department).
2. Any amendment to the plan for seating and other moveable furnishing, in accordance with [section 28-117.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-117.1).
3. Any change to the name of the establishment.



### **§28-117.2 Temporary Place of Assembly Certificate of Operation**

At the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner)'s discretion, a temporary certificate of operation may be issued for a place of assembly [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space) upon request by the applicant in accordance with this code provided that public safety is not jeopardized thereby. The applicant shall notify the fire [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) when a temporary place of assembly certificate of operation is issued.

**Exception.** Applications for temporary certificates of operation for place of assembly [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space) in [prior code buildings](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#prior_code_building) shall be permitted to comply with the [1968 building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-1968-v1) provided that public safety is not jeopardized thereby.

### **§28-117.3 Duration of Certificate**

A place of assembly certificate of operation shall be issued by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) and shall be effective for one year after its issuance.
