Thereafter, such certificate shall be effective only for periods of time during which there is in effect an annual place of assembly [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) issued by the fire [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) pursuant to section 105.6 of the [New York city fire code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-fire-code-2014).

### **§28-117.4 Security Guards**

In the case of a certificate holder that offers for sale food and/or beverages for on-[premises](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#premises) consumption, but not including establishments operated by a not-for-profit corporation, and employs or uses the services of a security guard, as that term is defined in subdivision six of section eighty-nine of the general business law, such certificate holder shall comply with the provisions of article 7-A of the general business law, shall obtain proof that such security guard is registered pursuant to article 7-A of the general business law, shall maintain such proof in a readily available location, in accordance with rules promulgated by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) during all hours in which such place of assembly is open to the public, shall maintain a roster of all security guards working at any given time when such place of assembly is open to the public, and shall require each security guard to maintain on his or her person proof of registration at all times when on the [premises](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#premises).

#### **§28-117.4.1 Presumption**

For purposes of this section, there shall be a rebuttable presumption that a person employed or whose services are retained at a place of assembly is a security guard if his or her job functions include:

1. The monitoring or guarding of the entrance or exit of such place of assembly to manage ingress and egress to such place of assembly for security purposes during the hours of operation of such establishment; and/or
2. Protection of such place of assembly from disorderly or other unlawful conduct by patrons of such place of assembly.



##### **§28-117.4.1.1 Presumption Not Applicable to Owner**

The rebuttable presumption in [section 28-117.4.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-117.4.1) shall not apply to an individual who is an [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of the establishment as described in [section 28-117.4](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-117.4) that has received a place of assembly certificate of operation.

#### **§28-117.4.2 Responsibility for Violations**

Notwithstanding any provision of this section, only the holder of a certificate of operation shall be liable for violations of this article that relate to such holder's obligations regarding security guards.

#### ***§28-117.4.3 Enforcement**

In addition to employees of the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department), employees of the police [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) and the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of consumer and worker protection shall have the authority to enforce the provisions of this article regarding security guards.

*Section 28-117.4.3 was amended by [Local Law 80 of 2020](http://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll80of2020.pdf). This law has an effective date of August 28, 2020.

#### **§28-117.4.4 State Liquor Authority Reporting**

The enforcement agency shall report any violation of the provisions of this section relating to security guards to the state liquor authority if the holder of the certificate of operation holds a [license](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#license) pursuant to the alcoholic beverage control law.

### **§28-117.5 Outdoor Places of Assembly**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall not issue a certificate of operation to an outdoor temporary or permanent place of assembly, including, but not limited to, tents, platforms, stages and outdoor assembly seating, unless the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) determines that the [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space) complies with the provisions of the code.

## **Article 118 Certificates of Occupancy**

### **§28-118.1 General Provisions**

No building or open lot shall be used or occupied without a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) issued by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner). Issuance of a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) shall not be construed as an approval of a violation of the provisions of this code or of other applicable laws and rules.

### **§28-118.2 New Buildings or Open Lots**

No building [hereafter](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#hereafter) constructed or open lot shall be occupied or used, in whole or in part, unless and until a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) shall have been issued certifying that such building or open lot conforms substantially to the approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and the provisions of this code and other applicable laws and rules.

### **§28-118.3 Completed Buildings or Open Lots**

The provisions of sections [28-118.3.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-118.3.1) through [28-118.3.4](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-118.3.4) shall apply to completed buildings or open lots.

#### **§28-118.3.1 Change of Occupancy or Use**

No building, open lot or portion thereof [hereafter](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#hereafter) altered so as to change from one [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) group to another, or from one zoning use group to another, either in whole or in part, shall be occupied or used unless and until the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) has issued a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) certifying that the [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) work for which the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) was issued has been completed substantially in accordance with the approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and the provisions of this code and other applicable laws and rules for the new [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) or use.

#### **§28-118.3.2 Changes Inconsistent With Existing Certificate of Occupancy**

No change shall be made to a building, open lot or portion thereof inconsistent with the last issued certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) or, where applicable, inconsistent with the last issued certificate of completion for such building or open lot or which would bring it under some special provision of this code or other applicable laws or rules, unless and until the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) has issued a new or amended certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy).

##### **§28-118.3.2.1 Changes in the Address, Block, Lot, or Zoning Lot**

When changes are made in the address of the structure, block and/or lot numbers or metes and bounds of the zoning lot that are inconsistent with the certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy), the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) shall obtain a new or amended certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) within one year.

#### **§28-118.3.3 Changes to Exits**

No building [hereafter](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#hereafter) altered so as to cause a major [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) to existing exits shall be occupied or used unless and until the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) has issued a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) certifying that the [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration) work for which the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) was issued has been completed substantially in accordance with the approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and the provisions of this code and other applicable laws and rules.

#### **§28-118.3.4 Existing Buildings or Open Lots Without Certificates of Occupancy**

A building or open lot in existence prior to January 1, 1938 and [heretofore](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#heretofore) legally used or occupied without a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) or, if applicable, a certificate of completion, and subject to the provisions of [section 28-102.4](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-102.4) (continuation of lawful existing use), may continue to be used or occupied without a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) or, if applicable, a certificate of completion, pursuant to the requirements of section six hundred forty five of the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) [charter](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#charter), this code and other applicable laws and rules provided there is no change in the existing use or [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) classification of the building, open lot or portion thereof.

##### **§28-118.3.4.1 Application for Certificate of Occupancy**

Upon application by the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of such a building or open lot in existence prior to January 1, 1938, the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall issue a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) for such building, provided that at the time of issuing such certificate, such existing building is in compliance with all retroactive requirements of the [1968 building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-1968-v1) applicable to such building and no notices of violation or other notices or orders affecting the building as they relate to the provisions of this code or the [1968 building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-1968-v1) are pending before the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department), and provided further that it is established to the satisfaction of the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner), after inspection and investigation, that the alleged use of the building has [heretofore](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#heretofore) legally existed.

##### **§28-118.3.4.2 Partial Certificates of Occupancy**

Partial certificates of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) may be issued pursuant to [section 28-118.16](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-118.16).

### **§28-118.4 Applications for Certificates of Occupancy**

All applications for certificates of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) shall be submitted on forms furnished by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). Applications for new buildings or [additions](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#addition) to buildings shall be accompanied by an accurate and complete final lot survey made by a [land surveyor](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#land_surveyor) showing such information as prescribed by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner). The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may waive the requirement of such survey in the case of small sheds, stands, temporary structures, [signs](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign), and similar small structures.

#### **§28-118.4.1 Applicant**

The application for a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) shall be made by or on behalf of the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of the building or open lot; and if made by a person other than the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner), the application shall be accompanied by a signed statement of the applicant stating that the applicant is authorized by the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) to make the application. The full names and addresses of the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner), and applicant, and of the principal officers thereof, if a corporation, shall be stated in the application.

#### **§28-118.4.2 Statement of Compliance**

When a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) for a new or altered building is applied for, the application shall be accompanied by a signed statement of the [registered design professional of record](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#registered_design_professional_of_record) or the [superintendent of construction](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#superintendent_of_construction), as applicable, stating that such person has examined the approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and specifications of the building for which the certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) is sought, and that, to the best of his or her knowledge and belief, the building has been erected or altered in accordance with the approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and specifications and, as erected or altered, complies with the provisions of this code and all other applicable laws and rules, except insofar as variations or variances therefrom have been legally permitted or authorized, specifying such variations or variances in such required statement.

### **§28-118.5 Review of Applications for Certificates of Occupancy**

All applications for certificates of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) and accompanying [submittal documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#submittal_documents) shall be examined promptly after their submission. If the building is entitled to the certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) applied for, the application shall be approved and the certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) issued by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) within 10 calendar days after submission of a complete application. Otherwise, the application shall be rejected and [written notice](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#written_notice) of rejection, stating the grounds of rejection, shall be given to the applicant within 10 calendar days of the submission of the application. Wherever an application has been rejected and proof is thereafter submitted establishing that the grounds of rejection have been met and that the building is entitled to the certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) applied for, the application shall be approved and the certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) issued within 10 calendar days after submission of such proof.

### **§28-118.6 Issuance of Certificate of Occupancy**

After the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) inspects the building or open lot and determines that the building or open lot conforms substantially to the approved [construction documents](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#construction_documents) and to the provisions of this code and other applicable laws and rules, the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall issue a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) that shall contain information including, but not limited to:

1. The building [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) number.
2. The address of the structure.
3. Block and lot numbers pertaining to the zoning lot as of the date of issuance, as defined in section 12-10 of the [New York city zoning resolution](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-zoning-resolution).
4. The description of the structure for which the certificate is issued.
5. A statement that the described portion of the structure has been inspected for compliance with the requirements of this code.
6. The name and signature of the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner).
7. The code under which the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) was issued.
8. The use and [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy), in accordance with this code and the [zoning resolution](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-zoning-resolution).
9. The type of construction as defined in this code.
10. The design occupant load of floors and [spaces](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space).
11. Types of major fire suppression or alarm systems.
12. Any special stipulations and conditions of the building [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit).
13. The maximum permissible live loads on the several floors of the building.
14. The number of parking [spaces](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space).



### **§28-118.7 Pavement Plan**

No certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) shall be issued for any building or open lot requiring a pavement plan pursuant to [article 108](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#108) unless and until an inspection has been made to show that all work necessary for compliance with the pavement plan has been completed.

#### **§28-118.7.1 Certification**

No certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) shall be issued for any building or open lot requiring a certification pursuant to [article 108](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#108) unless and until the applicant, after completion of construction work, inspects the sidewalk and certifies that the sidewalk is free from defects.

**Exception:** The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may issue a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) if in lieu of such certification the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) furnishes to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) prior to the issuance of the certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) security satisfactory to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) that the sidewalk will be installed and paved or repaired within the time specified by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department).

### **§28-118.8 Sanitary/Storm Water Drainage**

No certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) shall be issued until the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) confirms by inspection that all work relating to the installation of the part of the sanitary/storm water drainage system which lies outside of such property, if and as required by section 24-526 of the administrative code, has been satisfactorily completed.

### **§28-118.9 Fire Protection Plan**

No certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) shall be issued until a [fire protection plan](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#fire_protection_plan), if required pursuant to [article 109](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#109), has been filed and accepted.

### **§28-118.10 Electrical Work**

No certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) shall be issued unless compliance with the [New York city electrical code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-electrical-code-2011) is certified by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner).

### **§28-118.11 Certificates of Compliance**

No certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) shall be issued until [certificates of compliance](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#certificate_of_compliance) are issued for the following types of [service equipment](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#service_equipment):

1. Air conditioning and ventilation systems.
2. Elevators, escalators, moving walkways and dumbwaiters.
3. Fuel burning and fuel oil storage equipment.
4. Refrigeration systems.
5. Heating systems.
6. Boilers.



### **§28-118.12 Place of Assembly Certificate of Operation**

The issuance of a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) shall not authorize the use of any [space](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#space) as a place of assembly unless and until the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) thereafter issues a place of assembly certificate of operation.

### **§28-118.13 Certificates of Occupancy for Air-Inflated Structures, Air-Supported Structures, and Tents**

Certificates of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) for air-inflated structures, air-supported structures, and tents shall be issued for a period not exceeding one year. Such certificates may be renewed for one-year periods upon demonstration that the structure complies with all laws and rules in effect at the time of the request for renewal.

### **§28-118.14 Payment of Outstanding Penalties**

The [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) may refuse to issue a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) for a building pending payment of all outstanding fines or civil penalties imposed for violations of this code, the [1968 building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-1968-v1) or other laws enforced by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) at the same building.

### **§28-118.15 Temporary Certificates of Occupancy**

Upon application, the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) is authorized to issue a temporary certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) before the completion of the entire work covered by the [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit), provided that the subject portion or portions of the building may be occupied and maintained in a manner that will not endanger public safety, health, or welfare. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall set a time period during which the temporary certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) is valid.

### **§28-118.16 Amended Certificate of Occupancy**

The provisions of sections [28-118.16.1](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-118.16.1) through [28-118.16.2](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#§28-118.16.2) shall apply to amended certificates of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy).

#### **§28-118.16.1 Buildings Exceeding Three Stories in Height and Change Does Not Exceed 20 Percent of Total Floor Area**

Where a building exceeds three stories in height and the change does not exceed 20 percent of the total floor area, an amendment to the existing certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) for such new use shall be issued by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) certifying that the proposed new [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) and use conforms to the provisions of the laws governing building construction and that the proposed use will not be in conflict with any provisions of the labor law, [multiple dwelling law](https://up.codes/viewer/ny-multiple-dwelling-law) or the [zoning resolution](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-zoning-resolution).

#### **§28-118.16.2 Change in Address of the Structure, Block and Lot Numbers or Metes and Bounds of a Zoning Lot Subsequent to the Issuance of a Certificate of Occupancy**

Where no change is made to a building, open lot or portion thereof inconsistent with the last issued certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy), an amended certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) may be issued to reflect a change in the address of the structure, block and lot numbers or the metes and bounds of the zoning lot. Notwithstanding any other provisions of law, removal of violations and payments of outstanding penalties are not required prior to issuance of an amended certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) in accordance with this section 28-118.16.2.

### **§28-118.17 Revocation of Certificates of Occupancy**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) is authorized to request, in [writing](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#writing), pursuant to section six hundred forty five of the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) [charter](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#charter) that the board of standards and appeals or a court of competent jurisdiction revoke, vacate, or modify a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) issued under the provisions of this code whenever the certificate is issued in error, or on the basis of incorrect information provided to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department).

### **§28-118.18 Record of Certificates**

A record of all certificates of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) shall be kept by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department); and copies thereof shall be furnished by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) upon request, and on the payment of the fee prescribed in [article 112](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#112) of this chapter. The certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) or a copy thereof shall be available for inspection at the building at all reasonable times.

### **§28-118.19 Posting of Certificates of Occupancy**

The [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) shall post a copy of the building's certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) in accordance with this section 28-118.19, except buildings occupied entirely by group R3. Buildings that are not required to have a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) shall be posted by the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) with a [sign](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign) or placard in a form prescribed by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner). The certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) or [sign](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign), as applicable, shall be permanently affixed to the structure in a conspicuous location in a public hall, corridor, management office of the building or as otherwise prescribed by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner).

#### **§28-118.19.1 Replacement of Posted Certificates of Occupancy and Signs**

All posted certificates of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) or [signs](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign), as applicable, shall not be removed or defaced and, if lost, removed or defaced, shall be immediately replaced. The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may inspect or cause to be inspected periodically all buildings for compliance with the provisions of this code in regard to posting; and the inspection reports shall specify any violation thereof.

### **§28-118.20 Partial Certificate of Occupancy**

A partial certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) may be issued to a specific floor or floors of an existing building erected prior to January 1, 1938 subject to the following conditions:

1. The building does not have and is not otherwise required to have a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) or certificate of completion, if applicable.
2. The floor or floors for which a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) is issued shall not constitute more than 50 percent of the gross floor area of the building.
3. The building is of noncombustible construction and protected with an automatic sprinkler system.
4. Adequate means of egress are provided from all floors.
5. Upon inspection, the building is deemed safe for [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy).



### **§28-118.21 Live Loads Posted**

Where the live loads for which each floor or portion thereof of a commercial or industrial building is or has been designed to exceed 50 psf (2.40 kN/m2), a certificate of [occupancy](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#occupancy) required by this article shall not be issued until such design loads shall be conspicuously posted by the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) in that part of each story in which they apply, using durable [signs](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign). It shall be unlawful to remove or deface such [signs](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign).

**Exception:** This section 28-118.21 shall not apply to [prior code buildings](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#prior_code_building).

## **Article 119 Service Utilities**

### **§28-119.1 Connection of Service Utilities**

It shall be unlawful for any utility company or utility corporation to supply gas to a building, place or [premises](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#premises) in which new [meters](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#meter) other than replacement are required until a certificate of approval of gas installation from the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) is filed with such utility company or utility corporation. When new gas service piping has been installed it shall be locked-off by the utility company or utility corporation either by locking the gas service line valve or by installing a locking device on the outside gas service line valve. The lock shall not be removed until the gas [meter](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#meter) piping (other than utility owned) and gas distribution piping have been inspected and certified as required by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) of buildings as being ready for service.

#### **§28-119.1.1 Gas Shut-Off for Alterations to Gas Piping Systems**

When [alterations](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration), extensions or repairs to existing gas [meter](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#meter) piping or gas distribution piping require the shut-off of gas flow to a building, the utility company shall be notified by the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) or his or her authorized representative.

### **§28-119.2 Temporary Connection**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) shall have the authority to authorize the temporary connection of the building or system to the gas service utility.

### **§28-119.3 Authority to Disconnect Utility Service**

The [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner) may authorize disconnection of gas service to the building, structure or system regulated by this code and the codes referenced in case of emergency where necessary to eliminate an immediate hazard to life or property. The [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall notify the local gas utility company, and wherever possible the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) and occupant of the building, structure or service system of the decision to disconnect prior to taking such action.

### ***§28-119.4 Notification of Gas Shut-Off or Non-Restoration After Inspection**

Within 24 hours after gas service to a building is shut off by a utility company or utility corporation because of a class A or class B condition, as described in part 261 of title 16 of the New York codes, rules and regulations, and within 24 hours after gas service is, after an inspection by such a company or corporation, not restored because of such a condition, such company or corporation and the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of such building shall each provide notice to the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) in a form and manner prescribed by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department).

**Section 28-119.4 was added by [Local Law 154 of 2016](http://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll154of2016.pdf). This law has an effective date of March 6, 2017.*

## *** Article 120 Tenant Protection Plan**

*Article 28-120 was added by [Local Law 106 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll106of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of March 8, 2020.

### ***\**§28-120.1 Tenant Protection Plan**

A [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan shall be prepared and submitted for the [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration), construction, or [partial demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition_partial) of buildings in which any [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) will be occupied during construction, including newly constructed buildings that are partially occupied where work is ongoing. The [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan shall be prepared by a [registered design professional](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#registered_design_professional) and filed with the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). The [registered design professional](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#registered_design_professional) preparing the [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan shall be retained by the [general contractor](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/4/licensing-and-registration-of-businesses-trades-and-occupations-engaged-in-build#general_contractor) performing the [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration), construction, or [partial demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition_partial) work. No [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) shall be issued for work that requires a [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan unless such plan is approved by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department). Such plan shall contain a statement signed by the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) and signed by the applicant affirming that the building contains [dwelling units](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) that will be occupied during construction and shall identify in sufficient detail the specific units that are or may be occupied during construction, the means and methods to be employed to safeguard the safety and health of the occupants throughout the construction, including, where applicable, details such as temporary fire-rated assemblies, opening protectives, or dust containment procedures. Such means and methods shall be described with particularity and in no case shall terms such as "code compliant," "approved," "legal," "protected in accordance with law" or similar terms be used as substitute for such description. The [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan must be site specific. The elements of the [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan may vary depending on the nature and scope of the work but at a minimum, must comply with all applicable laws and regulations, including the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) construction codes, the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) housing maintenance code, the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) noise control code and the NewYork [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) health code, and shall make detailed and specific provisions for:

1. **Egress.** At all times in the course of construction provision shall be made for adequate egress as required by this code and the [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan shall identify the egress that will be provided. Required egress shall not be obstructed at any time except where approved by the [commissioner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#commissioner).

2. **Fire safety.** All necessary laws and controls, including those with respect to occupied dwellings, as well as additional safety measures necessitated by the construction shall be strictly observed.

3. Health requirements. 

   Specification of means and methods to be used for control of dust, disposal of construction debris, pest control and maintenance of sanitary facilities shall be included.

   3.1 There shall be included a statement of compliance with applicable provisions of law relating to lead and asbestos, and such statement shall describe with particularity what means and methods are being undertaken to meet such compliance.

4. **Compliance with housing standards.** The requirements of the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) housing maintenance code, and, where applicable, the [New York state multiple dwelling law](https://up.codes/viewer/ny-multiple-dwelling-law) shall be strictly observed.

5. **Structural safety.** No structural work shall be done that may endanger the occupants.

6. **Noise restrictions.** Specification of means and methods to be used for the limitation of noise to acceptable levels in accordance with the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) noise control code shall be included. Where hours of the day or the days of the week in which construction work may be undertaken are limited pursuant to the New York [city](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#city) noise control code, such limitations shall be stated.

7. **Maintaining essential services.** 

   Where heat, hot water, cold water, gas, electricity, or other utility services are provided in such building or in any dwelling unit located therein, the tenant protection plan shall specify the means and methods to be used for maintaining such services during such work in accordance with the requirements of the New York city housing maintenance code. If a disruption of any such service is anticipated during the work, then such plan shall specify the anticipated duration of such disruption and the means and methods to be employed to minimize such disruption, including the provision of sufficient alternatives for such service during such disruption. Notification of the disruption must be given to all affected occupants of occupied dwelling units.

   **Exception:** In the following instances, the tenant protection plan may be prepared and filed by the registered design professional of record for the alteration, construction, or partial demolition work as part of the underlying application:

   1. Work in occupied one-and two-family homes.
2. Work limited to the interior of a single [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) of an occupied multiple dwelling with no disruption to the essential services of other units, where such dwelling is [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner)-occupied. For a [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) within a property that is owned by a condominium or held by a shareholder of a [cooperative corporation](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#cooperative_corporation) under a proprietary lease, the unit must be occupied by the [owners](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of record for such unit.

*Section 28-104.8.4 was amended by [Local Law 154 of 2017](http://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll154of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of December 28, 2017.

**Section 28-104.8.4 was renumbered to 28-120.1 and amended by [Local Law 106 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll106of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of March 8, 2020.

***Section 28-120.1 was amended by [Local Law 116 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll116of2019.pdf) and [Local Law 118 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll118of2019.pdf). These laws have an effective date of March 8, 2020.

#### ***\*§28-120.1.1 Public Availability of Tenant Protection Plan**

Upon issuance of a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for work containing a [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan, the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) shall make the [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan publicly available on its website.

*Section 28-104.8.4.1 was added by [Local Law 154 of 2017](http://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll154of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of December 28, 2017.

**Section 28-104.8.4.1 was renumbered to 28-120.1.1 and amended by [Local Law 106 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll106of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of March 8, 2020.

***\*§28-120.1.2 Provision of Copy of Tenant Protection Plan to Occupants Upon Request**

The [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of a building undergoing work for which a [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan is required by section 28-120.1 shall, upon request from an occupant of a [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) within such building, provide such occupant with a paper copy of the [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan approved by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department).

*Section 28-104.8.4.2 was added by [Local Law 154 of 2017](http://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll154of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of December 28, 2017.

**Section 28-104.8.4.2 was renumbered to 28-120.1.2 and amended by [Local Law 106 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll106of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of March 8, 2020.

#### ***\*§28-120.1.3 Notice to Occupants**

Upon issuance of a [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) for work containing a [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan, the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) shall (i) distribute a notice regarding such plan to each occupied [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) and (ii) post a notice regarding such plan in a conspicuous manner in the building lobby, as well as on each floor within ten feet of the elevator, or in a building where there is no elevator, within ten feet of or in the main stairwell on such floor. The notice shall be in a form created or approved by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) and shall include:

1. A statement that occupants of the building may obtain a paper copy of such plan from the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) and may access such plan on the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) website;
2. The name and contact information for the site safety manager, site safety coordinator or [superintendent of construction](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#superintendent_of_construction) required by [section 3301.3](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014/chapter/33/safeguards-during-construction-or-demolition#*3301.3) of the [New York city building code](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-building-code-2014), as applicable, or, if there is no site safety manager, site safety coordinator or [superintendent of construction](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#superintendent_of_construction), the name and contact information of the [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner) of the building or such [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner)'s designee; and
3. A statement that occupants of the building may call 311 to make complaints about the work.

*Section 28-104.8.4.3 was added by [Local Law 154 of 2017](http://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll154of2017.pdf). This law has an effective date of December 28, 2017.

**Section 28-104.8.4.3 was renumbered to 28-120.1.3 and amended by [Local Law 106 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll106of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of March 8, 2020.

### ***§28-120.2 Phased Tenant Protection Plans**

Multiple layouts of the [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection features enumerated in section 28-120.1 may be submitted at any time during construction operations to show phased [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan designs consistent with the phase of anticipated work. Layouts submitted subsequent to a previously approved [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan shall constitute an amendment to such plan. Such amended plan shall be approved by the [department](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#department) prior to the commencement of the work requiring such amended plan.

*Section 28-120.2 was added by [Local Law 106 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll106of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of March 8, 2020.

### ***§28-120.3 Contractor Statement**

The [permit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#permit) holder for the underlying [alteration](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#alteration), construction, or [partial demolition](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#demolition_partial) shall [sign](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/5/miscellaneous-provisions#sign) a statement certifying that the [tenant](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#tenant) protection plan submitted by the [registered design professional](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/1/administration#registered_design_professional) coordinates with the scope of work intended.
Exception: This statement shall not be required for:

1. Work in occupied one-and two-family homes.
2. Work limited to the interior of a single [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) of an occupied multiple dwelling with no disruption to the essential services of other units, where such dwelling is [owner](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#owner)-occupied. For a [dwelling unit](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#dwelling_unit) within a property that is owned by a condominium or held by a shareholder of a [cooperative corporation](https://up.codes/viewer/new_york_city/nyc-general-administrative-provisions-2014/chapter/3/maintenance-of-buildings#cooperative_corporation) under a proprietary lease, the unit must be occupied by the owners of record for such unit.


*Section 28-120.3 was added by [Local Law 106 of 2019](https://www1.nyc.gov/assets/buildings/local_laws/ll106of2019.pdf). This law has an effective date of March 8, 2020.
